U.S. Congress to Discuss War Debts Next Week 27

Hoover hopes all countries will pay their debts on time

But suggests re-establishing the War Debt Revision Committee

Key British and French figures to meet in Paris today

Reuters, Paris, Sixth Day - According to sources in Geneva, British Prime Minister MacDonald and French President Herriot are expected to arrive here tomorrow. British Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain will also arrive in Paris tomorrow. Thus, there is an indication that a debt conference will be held here between Britain and France. The House of Representatives will begin debating the debt issue on Friday or Saturday. The House opposes payment, while Herriot advocates payment.

National News Agency, Rome, Fifth Day - The Italian Fascist Grand Council today issued a communique endorsing the resolution that Italy should pay the U.S. war debt due on December 15th as scheduled, and immediately begin negotiations on a new war debt agreement. It is reported that the total amount due by Italy this time is 1,245,437 gold dollars. It is said that the Italian government can raise cash for payment. As for the new agreement, the communique advocates that it should be concluded before the next due date of June 15th next year.

War Debt Case Postponed 28

Hoover hopes all countries will pay their debts on time

Reuters, New York, Sixth Day - According to the New York Times' Washington correspondent, President Hoover has changed his plan. His message to Congress regarding the war debt issue will be delayed until the latter half of this week. According to official sources, the message will address disarmament and the World Economic Conference, as President Hoover believes these two facts are related to the war debt issue.

Reuters, Washington, Fifth Day - President Hoover's message to Congress will only briefly mention war debts and intends to postpone the matter until December 15th for discussion. At that time, he will suggest re-establishing the War Debt Repayment Committee to consider revising the debt situation. President Hoover still hopes that all countries will pay the amount due on December 15th as scheduled.

Repeal of Prohibition Rejected 29

To be reintroduced after Roosevelt takes office

National News Agency, Washington, Fifth Day - The U.S. Congress opened today, but the repeal of the Prohibition Amendment failed to pass the House of Representatives by a margin of five votes. Those in favor received 271 votes, while those opposed received 144 votes. These 144 people all represent electoral districts that advocate Prohibition and are expected to continue to oppose the case. Therefore, even if the case can be reintroduced during this short session, the hope of its passage is very slim. As for the relaxation of the beer ban, according to Speaker of the House Garner, he will still urge its rapid progress to ensure its passage as soon as possible. The Senate opened today, held a prayer ceremony and a new senator oath ceremony, and then adjourned in mourning for the senators who died during the recess.

National News Agency, Hot Springs, Fifth Day - President-elect Roosevelt did not express any opinion on today's failure of the House of Representatives to pass the resolution to repeal the Prohibition Amendment. However, Democratic leaders who came here to discuss the issue with Roosevelt believe that Roosevelt will propose the case to a special session of Congress after taking office. According to sources in Washington, the special session of Congress, in view of the recent progress in national industry and commerce and the gradual decrease in unemployment, originally did not seem likely to be convened. However, due to the repeal of the Prohibition Amendment, it has been decided to convene it. It is also heard that the Democrats now believe that although the case failed to pass due to the lack of a two-thirds majority, the party's promise to the voters has already been fulfilled, and the matter can be handled again after the new congressmen are sworn in.

The Capitol is Closed to Outsiders to Prevent Undesirable Actions by Unemployed Petitioners 30

Reuters, Washington, Fifth Day - The Capitol is closed to outsiders for fear that unemployed petitioners will take undesirable actions.

Spain to Nationalize All Telegraph and Telephone Services 31

The U.S. government lodges a protest with the Spanish government to protect American commercial assets

National News Agency, Washington, Fifth Day - A serious diplomatic situation may arise between the United States and Spain. The Spanish Congress is currently discussing a government proposal to nationalize all telephone and telegraph services. However, the proposal does not include any provisions for compensation. The American International Telephone and Telegraph Company has laid long-distance telephone lines throughout Spain, as well as wireless communication with South America, and has established a telephone factory in Santander and a cable factory in Madrid, estimated to be worth 65 million gold dollars. Therefore, Under Secretary of State Castle today specifically told Spanish Ambassador Pierra that if the Spanish Congress passes the bill in its current form after the American International Telephone and Telegraph Company's assets are taken back, the United States will notify the Spanish government to demand full compensation for damages. If the Spanish government refuses to negotiate, the United States will not hesitate to withdraw its ambassador to Spain. Pierra replied that the Spanish president believes that this case is purely a domestic matter and does not involve the United States. Castle stated that the U.S. government believes that if American assets are confiscated anywhere, the government should negotiate on its behalf to obtain compensation. It is now heard that Pierra has telegraphed the U.S. government's attitude to his home country and is awaiting a reply.

Japanese Cabinet Overthrow Movement: The Resolution of the Seiyukai's Hardliners 34

▲ Den Tsushin, Tokyo, Sixth Day - The two major meetings of the Seiyukai, which advocate for the overthrow of the current cabinet, and the meeting of concerned Diet members directly under President Suzuki, which includes a continuing self-restraint attitude, were held last night at the Hibiya Taotao Pavilion. More than fifty people, including Uehara Etsujiro, Ando Masazumi, Miyakawa Ikkaku, Ito Jintaro, and Isobe Hei, attended. Advisor Hirose Tametsugu was elected as chairman. It was also decided to recruit all party members in the near future to hold a meeting of concerned Diet members to expand and strengthen the movement toward party justice and unanimously overthrow the cabinet.

Japanese Cruiser Hayasuzu Sinks: 106 Officers and Soldiers Drown 35

Den Tsushin, Tokyo, Sixth Day - The Hayasuzu, which suffered the disaster, belongs to the Thirteenth Destroyer Squadron and has four ships: Wakatake, Gotake, Sanae, and Hayasuzu. This time, it was replacing the Twenty-Fifth Destroyer Squadron. The Hayasuzu was responsible for guarding the Makung Naval Port. It departed from the Kure Naval Port for Makung on December 2nd, which led to the disaster. The cruisers Kitakami and Isuzu have been dispatched from Makung to the scene to provide assistance. The mainland is not dispatching ships for rescue. According to the Navy Ministry's announcement at midnight this morning, the distress signal was received from the destroyer team on the scene at 8 pm last night. The hull of the Hayasuzu was lost in the dark. The destroyer team continued to do its best in the search. The ship's crew includes Captain Lieutenant Commander Kadota Kengo, Lieutenant Commander Michiki Katsura, Lieutenant Yamazaki Takashi, Ensign Shimizu Sadao, Engineer Lieutenant Commander Miura Fumitoku, Warrant Officer Yamazaki Teizo, Paymaster Lieutenant Commander Yano Hideo, and Medical Corps Lieutenant Rikioka Tokutaro. There are a total of ten officers and warrant officers and above, and one hundred and nine enlisted men. Among them, fourteen were rescued by allied ships, and the remaining one hundred and six are likely hopeless.

Five Great Powers' Disarmament Conference 61

England, America, France, and Italy Agreed on the Details of the American Plan

German Representative Asks for a Few Days to Respond

Reuters, Geneva, Sixth Day - Last night's dinner party by British Prime Minister MacDonald failed to yield any resolution from Germany. The British Prime Minister stated to German Foreign Minister Neurath that there was absolutely no anti-German united front. The German Foreign Minister asked for a few days to respond. This morning, the five major powers will have another meeting. French Premier Herriot is scheduled to return to Paris tonight, but can return to Geneva on Saturday or Sunday if necessary.

Reuters, Geneva, Fifth Day - Whether the plan proposed by the United States, which is equivalent to a recess of the disarmament conference, can be accepted by Germany is currently an important issue. The United States advocates that all countries must sign a document before December 15th listing the principles that each country can agree to, such as the abolition of chemical and microbial warfare, restrictions on artillery and tanks, and the prohibition of aerial bombardment. If Germany accepts this proposal, a supervisory committee will be established to replace the disarmament conference to carry out designated tasks within a limited period. However, whether Germany will accept it is still undetermined, and there may be some opposition from the small countries. During the meeting today, representatives from England, France, America, and Italy have agreed on the details of the American plan, which is nearing completion but still awaits Germany's acceptance. British Prime Minister MacDonald invited the chief representatives of the countries concerned, such as German Foreign Minister Neurath, to a dinner party tonight. It is generally believed that the British Prime Minister will try to persuade Germany to accept the American plan.

Havas, Geneva, Fifth Day - Today, the British Prime Minister convened representatives from England, France, and Italy to discuss the disarmament issue. Shortly after, German Foreign Minister Neurath arrived here, and MacDonald temporarily excused the representatives to meet with Neurath alone. Tonight, the representatives of the major powers will hold a group meeting.

Havas, Geneva, Fifth Day - Tomorrow, representatives from England, France, America, and Italy will meet with German Foreign Minister Neurath to discuss the issue of the disarmament conference reconvening. Today, British Prime Minister MacDonald invited representatives from France, America, and Italy twice, in the morning and afternoon, to discuss the procedure for the talks with Neurath tomorrow. Today's talks were purely in the form of free expression of opinions, and the representatives did not make any decisions until tomorrow. Therefore, no conclusions were reached. According to reports, the disarmament conference has entered a stalemate since Germany withdrew. Davis's plan may be able to save it. The representatives are carefully considering the possible consequences of this plan. The French delegation does not seem to oppose the principles advocated by Davis, but only on the condition that the preliminary agreement does not harm security. However, what kind of reaction will the German side have if this plan is put into practice? If German Foreign Minister Neurath demands that all countries immediately guarantee equality of armaments, what will be the result? All of these are of great concern to the French delegation. After German Foreign Minister Neurath arrived here, he spoke with the British Prime Minister for an hour. Unofficial talks between the five countries' representatives (including the German representative) will begin tonight, as MacDonald has invited them to dinner at his residence tonight. The official meeting will continue tomorrow.

Havas, Geneva, Fifth Day - The Japanese delegation to the Disarmament Conference recently formally submitted the Japanese naval proposal to French disarmament representative Poncet. According to reports, this proposal is part of Japan's qualitative disarmament plan, advocating reducing the offensive power of the navy and increasing its defensive power.

National News Agency, Geneva, Fifth Day - The Japanese delegation today notified the signatory countries of the Washington Disarmament Conference. Although the contents of the notification will not be made public until a few days later, according to those who know the contents, some of the treaties include reducing the tonnage of battleships from 35,000 tons to 15,000 tons, limiting or completely abolishing the number of aircraft carriers, and reserving 8-inch caliber guns for self-defense on all warships and submarines.

National News Agency, Geneva, Sixth Day - It is rumored that the talks between British Prime Minister MacDonald and German Foreign Minister Neurath last night have achieved some degree of reconciliation. Other sources claim that France, England, and the United States have agreed to postpone the disarmament conference for three years, and it is expected that Germany will also agree to shelve its demands for equality in disarmament during this period. This morning, German political circles claimed that Neurath never agreed to such a perfunctory approach and regretted that the Foreign Minister had been lured to Geneva only to confront the anti-German united front and promote the current situation in Europe according to France's wishes.

Soviet Russia's Cotton and Oil: Cotton Land Increased Threefold in Five Years, Oil Accounts for 30% of the World's Supply 62

Moscow, TASS, 5th - According to statistics released here today, the Soviet Union's cotton cultivation area has increased threefold in the past five years. In 1927, the cotton cultivation area was 2,005,250 acres, increasing to 3,814,750 acres in 1930, and further increasing to 5,870,500 acres in 1932. The Education Committee and Drama Society of Uzbekistan, the center of the cotton industry, have launched a drama competition to select a script depicting the Soviet cotton industry's independence from foreign supply.

Moscow, TASS - The total output of the Soviet oil industry in the first nine months of this year was 16,570,000 tons, compared to 22,300,000 tons in 1931, and only 9,200,000 tons in Old Russia in 1903. Oil has now become the most developed industry in the Soviet Union, with the opening of new oil fields increasing daily. The Bibi-Heybat Bay area in the Caspian Sea has been developed into a very rich oil field. The development of oil fields in Grozny, Maikop, and other places has also progressed. It is currently estimated that the Soviet Union contains 30% to 35% of the world's oil reserves and will inevitably develop into the world's leading oil producing country in the future. In recent years, the Soviet Union's investment in the oil industry has been considerable. Before the revolution, the Azneft refineries produced less than 3 million tons of oil, but by 1932, this had increased to 11.3 million tons. Grozny refined only 392,000 tons of oil in 1913, but this has now increased to 8 million tons. The percentage of oil extraction has also increased, from 2.7% for light oil in 1913 to 13.4% in 1932. The work of the Soviet oil industry has now been completely mechanized and electrified. The rotary drilling rig was invented by the Soviet engineer Kapelushnikov, and its drilling speed has increased from 30 to 40 meters per month in 1913 to 120 meters. Soviet oil merchants mainly supply domestic use, but exports have also increased two and a half times from 1926 to 1931.

The War Between Sichuan and Guizhou Provinces is Difficult to Stop 64

Sichuan War: The Allied Forces Will Attack Chengdu

Guizhou War: Guiyang and Zunyi Are Both Fierce

Chongqing Airmail - The war situation in Sichuan Province currently seems to be tending towards quiescence, with battles on all fronts slowly advancing. The vanguard of the 20th Army has reached Jingyan and is confronting the 24th Army in Jiading, without any fierce battles. The six counties of Xuzhou Prefecture, Qingfu, Changning, Gaoxian, Gongxian, Xingwen, and Junlian, have been successively occupied by the 21st Army. On the other hand, the two divisions of the 20th Army, the Tang Division, have occupied Renshou and are confronting the 24th Army. In the Zizhong and Jianyang areas, the three divisions of Li Qixiang, Yang Sen, and Luo Zezhou are also advancing to assist Deng Xihou and Tian Songyao. They have reached Chadianchang and Longquanyi (60 li from Chengdu) and are confronting the 24th Army. The 28th and 29th Armies, which withdrew from Chengdu, are now concentrated in Xindu (40 li from Chengdu), Hanzhou (90 li from Chengdu), Jintang, Shifang, and other counties, with a total strength of 60,000 men. When Li Qixiang, Yang Sen, Luo Zezhou, and the 20th Army approach Chengdu, they will lead their troops to counterattack and join forces in Chengdu. The 24th Army of Liu Wenhui has concentrated 60,000 to 70,000 men in Chengdu, preparing to defend the city. It is reported that on the 1st of this month, Liu Wenhui sent a telegram to Liu Xiang, appealing to their familial ties and mutual interests, stating that at a time when the country is facing difficulties and the situation in Kangzang is tense, it is truly shameful and despised by the world, and a great disgrace to the Liu family, that we two uncles and nephews are engaged in civil war. Now that my nephew has obtained the southern Sichuan defense area, he should be content and stop the military action and no longer force his uncle to solve the Deng Xihou and Tian Songyao issue (it is said that Deng Xihou and Liu Wenhui are both from the Baoding Military Academy. In this Sichuan war, Liu made many concessions to Deng, but Deng still raised troops to force him, so Liu was very angry and considered him an irreconcilable enemy). He further stated that he would lead his troops to be at his nephew's disposal, otherwise, his uncle would be forced to hand over his troops to Deng Xihou. In the future, if Deng Xihou's strength is sufficient, it will not be a blessing for his nephew either. Liu Xiang has not yet made any definite response. On the other hand, Tian Songyao also sent a telegram to Liu Xiang, saying, "The telegrams of truce and peace sent by the generals of the 24th, 28th, and 29th Armies are purely fabricated by Liu Wenhui. Songyao and Jin Kang have always stood on the side of the Allied Forces to jointly resolve the Sichuan situation. We are now concentrating our troops to prepare a counterattack and hope to join forces to take Chengdu." It is not yet known how Liu Xiang replied, but on the 30th of last month, Liu Xiang's planes dropped leaflets in Chengdu, ordering the people of Chengdu to evacuate beyond 20 li from the city within a week to avoid danger. It can be seen that the Allied Forces will join forces to attack Chengdu, which will become a reality, and the great battle will be on the Chengdu front in the future.

In Guizhou Province, after generals such as Che Mingyi and Jiang Zaizhen united and sent a joint telegram urging Wang Jialie to step down, hand over the provincial government, and for Mao Guangxiang to come out of retirement and resume his position as commander of the 25th Army, Wang Jialie was very angry and immediately sent the two independent brigades of Jian Wenbo and Li Chengzhang to attack the Third Division of Jiang Zaizhen stationed in Zunyi. Both sides fought fiercely at Wujiang, with each side suffering more than a thousand casualties. Vice Army Commander You Guocai then led his Second Division from Anshun and seized Guiyang by surprise. Wang Jialie, seeing the momentum was strong and difficult to resist, led his troops to withdraw from Guiyang and concentrated his forces in the vicinity to prepare for battle. First, he sent a telegram to You Guocai, expressing his willingness to cooperate jointly to manage the Guizhou situation. He was willing to hand over the position of chairman to You and combine the two forces to attack Jiang Zaizhen and Che Mingyi to stop Mao Guangxiang from resuming his position. You replied, proposing three conditions: 1. Wang Jialie must hand over the chairmanship and welcome Mao Guangxiang to resume his position. 2. Wang Jialie must hand over the command of the 25th Army to him, and he will hand over the position of vice army commander to Jiang Zaizhen or Che Mingyi. 3. Wang Jialie will serve as the commander of the training division and cooperate jointly, with other troops under the command of the commander of the 25th Army. Wang Jialie believed that You's conditions were too harsh and difficult to accept and refused. In recent days, the war situation on both sides of Guiyang and Wujiang has suddenly become fierce. The generals who supported Wang, such as He Zhiyong, Jian Wenbo, and Li Chengzhang, also sent a telegram supporting Wang's position as commander of the 25th Army and You Guocai's position as chairman, opposing Mao Guangxiang's return to power. Therefore, You had a tendency to soften. At the same time, Hou Zhidan, who was against Wang, was appointed by Liu Xiang of the 21st Army as the commander of the Guizhou-Sichuan border defense and expressed that he would not participate in the Guizhou war, but still urged Mao to come out of retirement and govern, based on his original intention of opposing Wang and supporting Mao. Jiang Zaizhen, Che Mingyi, Song Xing, and Hou Yujiu had disputes over the distribution of positions after the overthrow of Wang Jialie. Jiang and Che both wanted to be the commander of the 25th Army, while Song wanted the training division, and Hou coveted the First Division. He Zhiyong's troops, therefore, caused the anti-Wang group to split. Wang Jialie saw this situation and thought there was an opportunity to take advantage of, so he transferred He Zhiyong's First Division, stationed in Hongjiang, to concentrate in Guiyang to counterattack, and ordered Jian Wenbo and Li Chengzhang to attack Jiang Zaizhen fiercely in order to fight for the final victory. The Guizhou affairs are still in chaos, and there is no hope of a solution for the time being (November 3rd).

Puppet Discrimination Against Foreigners

Foreigners Feel They Cannot Establish Themselves in Manchuria, Very Difficult to Import Goods 65

The North-China Daily News, Harbin Correspondence, November 22nd - Lately, foreigners in Manchuria have been subjected to discrimination. Mr. Sugihara, the Japanese representative of the "Manchukuo" Foreign Ministry stationed in Harbin, said to the representative of the local Russian newspaper that the Changchun government has decided that all foreigners, including those with consular jurisdiction, will not be allowed to enter the country unless their passports have been properly visaed by the "Manchukuo" government. Previously, foreigners arriving without a visa were only warned, but from now on, they must comply with the passport regulations before being allowed to enter the country. Regarding this matter, an American recently held a passport and requested the Japanese Consulate in this city to visa it in order to return to his country via Japan, but was refused. The reason given was that it had not been visaed by the "Manchukuo" authorities, and it was claimed that this was at the request of the "Manchukuo" authorities. In fact, the two sides are one and the same. It is evident that the purpose of these two incidents is to force the recognition of various countries. This kind of coercion is now common. Foreign businessmen are being subjected to differential treatment and have little chance of competing with Japanese businessmen, who are given priority in everything. Currently, the customs offices no longer post notices in English. According to customs officials, they can only publish notices in Chinese, Japanese, and Russian, and refuse to send notices to merchants, saying that they can read Russian newspapers. Furthermore, inland navigation is completely monopolized by Japanese transportation companies. The South Manchuria Railway also only provides various conveniences to Japanese merchants. In addition, the Vladivostok line is now completely blocked, making it very difficult for British, American, and German merchants to transport goods into Manchuria. In short, it is still a long way off for foreign businessmen to have good hopes for trade in Manchuria.

Li Division Stationed in Xuzhou Transferred to Yichang 66

Xu Tingyao's Division Takes Over Defense of Xuzhou

Xuzhou Correspondence - The Ninth Division, commanded by Division Commander Li Yiannian, has been defending the area around Xubu and Dangshan. Now, Division Commander Li has received a telegram from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek ordering his troops to go to Hubei to defend Yichang and the western Hubei area. After Liu Xiang's troops returned to Sichuan, the vacant defense urgently needs to be filled, and the banditry along the Yangtze River should also be guarded against. As for the Xu defense, the Fourth Division, commanded by Division Commander Xu Tingyao, has been ordered to send a unit to take over the defense. After receiving the order, Li immediately notified the Jinpu Railway to prepare 13 trains for transportation. On the morning of the 5th, the independent brigade of the Fourth Division, commanded by Guan Linzheng, arrived in Xubu. The Ninth Division also began to go south on the empty trains that day. According to the plan, the Ninth Division was scheduled to send four trains on the 5th for the 26th Brigade, commanded by Zheng Zuomin, and the replenishment regiment, commanded by Wu Bin. Four trains were scheduled to be sent on the 7th for the division headquarters and direct subordinate units. Four trains were scheduled to be sent on the 9th for the 25th Brigade, commanded by Li Xiangrong. Finally, a train of baggage cars will be sent to complete the transportation. All trains will be transferred at Pukou and go directly to Yichang. Li Yiannian is scheduled to leave Xuzhou on the 6th and go south. This morning (the 5th), he invited representatives from all walks of life to a farewell gathering at the garrison headquarters, attended by 20 or 30 heads of various groups and institutions. Li reported that the division's stationing in Xuzhou has been deeply supported by the local people, and he is ashamed of not having made any achievements. In recent months, the division has paid special attention to the suppression of drugs, knowing that the spread of drugs is infinitely harmful and can be exploited by the communists. After the division leaves Xuzhou, he still hopes that all sectors of society will work hard to eliminate drugs and that they will be able to unite and govern themselves. The Fourth Division stationed in Xuzhou will be the same as the Ninth Division, cooperating with local construction. It should be known that no matter which army is stationed in which area, they all hope to make achievements and implement the purpose of mutual assistance between the army and the people. The representatives also made speeches in reply, and then dispersed after tea and refreshments. As for the Fourth Division troops arriving in Xuzhou, the cavalry regiment arrived at dawn this morning (the 5th) and immediately transferred to Dangshan so that the Ninth Division troops stationed there could depart. Independent Brigade Commander Guan Linzheng then led the brigade headquarters to arrive in Xuzhou by train at 7:00 this morning. Guan got off the train and temporarily stayed at the Oriental Hotel. According to Guan's conversation, the brigade was stationed in Fengyang after suppressing bandits in northern Anhui. Now it is ordered to open to Xuzhou. He boarded the train at Mentai zi and went north. Division Commander Xu is still guarding the Jinpu southern section along the line in Bengbu. The line is currently very peaceful, and the bandit areas in northern Anhui have also gradually recovered their former appearance. The brigade will continue to depart north on six trains and will be transported to completion that day. It is said that Guan plans to move to the police headquarters and city defense after Li Yiannian leaves, and Guan has sent a team to take over the post (5th).

Closing Arguments in Hu Lifu Case, Sentencing Set for 12th 67

The Jiangsu High Court heard the traitor Hu Lifu case at 2:00 p.m. today (the 6th). There were many people in the audience. Judge Hu Shangu, the presiding judge of the Second Criminal Tribunal, judges Zhang Bingci and Zhao Zongzhou, Prosecutor Zhu Wenzhuo, and Clerk 丨 Mou were in the First Criminal Tribunal to hear the case. Lawyer Wang Jian appeared in court to defend Hu. Witness Cheng Wenyan, the Chief Inspector of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, did not arrive. The arguments concluded and sentencing was set for the 12th. Hu cried during the signing and requested further investigation. A detailed record of the situation is as follows:

At around 1:00 p.m. today, Hu Lifu was first brought from the prison to the High Court and sat upright in the criminal waiting room, looking very relaxed. At 2:00 p.m., Hu Shangu, judge of the Second Criminal Tribunal, judges Zhang Bingci and Zhao Zongzhou, Prosecutor Shi Wenzhuo, and Clerk 丨 and others ascended to the First Court. (Question) Hu, what is your age, place of origin, and address? (Answer) 52 years old, Yongjia, Zhejiang, originally lived in Miaotou, Pengpu Town, later moved to Weihaiwei Road. (Question) When did you move there? (Answer) Around the January 28th Incident. (Question) What is your occupation? (Answer) I opened the Hecheng Tanning and Hydrating Factory on Binlang Road. (Question) How did you know Washizaki? (Answer) He is an engineer in the factory. (Question) How many years have you employed him? (Answer) Four years already. (Question) How is your relationship? (Answer) Not bad. (Question) Is the factory still open? (Answer) It is closed. (Question) Why is it closed? (Answer) Because of the January 28th Incident. (Question) Where did Washizaki go? (Answer) He moved to Hongkou. (Question) What was the situation with the Maintenance Association? (Answer) After the 19th Route Army defended the second line, around March 2nd or 3rd, my house was robbed and looted, and robberies occurred everywhere else. The people were in deep water and could not escape the disaster, so I organized the Maintenance Association to maintain order in the area. (Question) How many items were robbed from your house? (Answer) There were more than 40 leather suitcases. When I returned home, people nearby said that this place had been occupied by the Japanese army, and I could not escape. (Question) What happened later? (Answer) I went to see which army it was (Hu sobbed and could not speak), knowing it was the Japanese army, but there were dead bodies piled up everywhere, and some people were miserable and could not escape. So I organized the Maintenance Association. (Question) What did the Japanese think? (Answer) They also agreed and found a few assistants to organize the Northern District Maintenance Association. The work was quite successful because there were often refugees fleeing to the concession, and we protected them. (Question) So the meaning of organizing this association was the Japanese's meaning? (Answer) It was not the meaning of the merchants, it was the meaning of the people. (Question) There were Japanese people present at the time, how could it be the meaning of the merchants? (Answer) It was all lies from the Public Security Bureau and the newspapers. (Question) When was the Northern District Maintenance Association established? (Answer) It was established on April 1st. (Question) Did you get permission from the Japanese? (Answer) No, but I notified them. (Question) Did you report to the Municipal Government and the Chamber of Commerce? (Answer) I did report. (Question) How did you report it? (Answer) By official letter. (Question) When did you send the official letter? (Answer) I forgot the date. (Question) Organizing a Maintenance Association must be approved by the Municipal Government before it can be organized. According to you, it is an illegal organization. (Answer) When I reported it, the Municipal Government had already issued an arrest warrant, so there was no approval reply. (Question) The court has already investigated that there was no such thing as reporting to the Municipal Government and the Chamber of Commerce. At this point, the judge showed Hu the letter from the Municipal Government to the High Court and said that the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau received a report that this illegal organization immediately sent personnel to investigate secretly. After the report, Mayor Wu sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and President Wang in Nanjing. (Question) In short, in the enemy-occupied area, the association could not be established without the enemy's permission, and without the approval of the Municipal Government, the illegal attitude of the organization was very obvious. (Answer) That is Chinese territory, and there were disaster victims everywhere, with piles of corpses, and bandits took the opportunity to loot. The goods in the warehouses in Zhabei were worth tens of millions of dollars. If we didn't organize a Maintenance Association, not only would the people's property be looted, but the corpses would not be collected and buried in the warm weather at that time, which would be a great hindrance to hygiene. What's more, I witnessed the Chinese being humiliated by the Japanese. (Question) According to Telegram No. from the Shanghai Municipal Government, you were the chairman of the Northern District Citizens Maintenance Association, Wang Du was the vice chairman. The association was divided into six groups, with the Japanese Washizaki and Yokota as directors of the General Affairs Group, Vice Chairman Wang Du concurrently serving as director of the Finance Group, Chang Yuqing as director of the Patrol Police Group, Cheng Xiangbai as director of the Transportation Group, Yao Zhirui as director of the Investigation Group, and 丨 Qingyuan as director of the Hygiene Group, with 150 policemen under the command of Chang Yuqing and 50 detectives. (Answer) Wang Du escaped after a few days, and the rest of the organization and so on were all exaggerated by the newspapers. In fact, they did not understand the situation in the North District. (Question) The Municipal Government's telegram to Nanjing cannot be fabricated. (Question)

Did you hear him speak in English? (Answer) Yes. At this point, the officer read out Hu's statement to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. (Question) When was the Maintenance Association dissolved? (Answer) April 11th. (Question) Was it because the League of Nations intervened and the Japanese army dissolved the Maintenance Association? (Answer) No, we stopped doing it ourselves. (Question) When were you arrested? (Answer) August 16th. I was arrested at the Xin Yanlou restaurant on North Sichuan Road. There were many detectives secretly hiding with guns. I asked them if they had official business. They said they didn't care. At that time, everyone thought I was a Japanese traitor, and it was useless to argue. I went with them. I was being attacked on all sides because the Japanese also hated me. (Question) What was the name of the commander of the Fourth Battalion of the Japanese army? (Answer) His name was Yamashita. The commander-in-chief was Uematsu. (Question) What about Yokota and Washizaki? (Answer) They were interpreters for the Japanese. (Question) Did the Fourth Battalion come to investigate? (Answer) They came to investigate. (Question) It can be seen that it was organized according to the Japanese. (Answer) It was organized according to the Chinese, and it was a charitable organization. (Question) You once confessed that you were doing things according to the Fourth Battalion, but sometimes you had to do things according to your own. (Answer) No, I didn't. (Question) So you were appointed by the Japanese? (Answer) I was not appointed by the Japanese. I didn't set fires or loot. It was entirely a charitable organization. (Question) You also said that there were hundreds of people in the association during the investigation. (Answer) They were coolies because they were moving goods from the warehouses. (Question) In any case, why didn't you ask the government for approval? (Answer) Judge, please be aware that it takes a long time for the government to handle things. If we waited for approval, the area would have been ruined long ago. Don't we want our Chinese territory? The government didn't take care of it, so how can you blame us? (Question) You collected more than 3,000 yuan in taxes during the 10 days of the Maintenance Association's existence? (Answer) There was no so-called taxation. It was voluntary donations. (Question) You estimated the value of the goods and collected 2%? (Answer) No, otherwise I would have been detained for three or four months. Why didn't they come to accuse me earlier? (Question) Were the donation tickets issued by you? (Answer) They were just certificates for the circulation of goods. (Question) Did you receive a salary as chairman? (Answer) None at all, not even a penny. (Question) What kind of goods were transported out? (Answer) Kerosene, etc., were all things from the warehouses. (Question) The Japanese army estimated that Zhabei needed supplies, so you established this association to serve them. (Answer) No, the Japanese army sent many male and female inspectors at that time, distributing them at various intersections. Women had to be stripped and checked when entering and exiting, which damaged the national integrity. For the sake of the overall national integrity, I was absolutely not serving the Japanese. Moreover, the association was organized after the January 28th Incident, not before, so it was not serving the Japanese. (Question) So what was the purpose of the detectives and police? (Answer) There really weren't any. Otherwise, when I was escorted to Nanjing, wouldn't I have been shot immediately? I am a law-abiding businessman. My hair is already white and I have grandchildren. Why would I do anything illegal? (Question) What about the Yunhe Company? (Answer) I didn't ask or hear about the Yunhe Company. (Question) Who organized the company? (Answer) It was organized by Yokota. (Question) The Yunhe Company opened opium dens, sold opium, gambled, and collected commissions? (Answer) All of them are destructive. It only provides insurance and collects rent for others as its business. (Question) Your case has been thoroughly investigated by the authorities. (Answer) They are all lies fabricated by the detectives. (Question) Why would they fabricate rumors about you? (Answer) Because there are vested interests. (Question) It is conceivable that you have done such a thing. (Answer) The situation is opaque and I cannot publish a statement in the newspaper. (Question) Cheng Ruowen, also known as Zheng Yiyuan, of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, met you and knew that you were divided into several groups and established branches. The association had more than 20 staff members, and there were 20 or 30 long-term police officers. The Hongzhen branch was dissolved when the Japanese army was about to withdraw. The Yunhe Company was opened and collected more than 9,000 yuan. Do you understand? (Answer) It is a matter of my conscience. Why didn't I take the opportunity to rob? I was really doing it for the local people. (Question) Is the pistol yours? (Answer) It has a passport number from the National Government and the Municipal Government, number 27147. (Question) Liang, the director of the Shanghai Finance Bureau's donation collection, issued an investigation. According to the report of Li Jiqing, a patrol officer of the former Fourth District Public Security Bureau (the location of the Maintenance Association), two policemen with guns were guarding the area. (Answer) They were watchmen. At this point, the officer repeatedly stated that organizing a group in the Japanese-occupied area without government approval was illegal. Hu replied that he remembered that when the French territory was occupied by Germany, the French also came out to maintain order. In short, the people now hate the Japanese deeply, so they hate me. Hu Lifu said that I am a traitor, but the people will not hate me if they know the inside story. At this point, the judge asked if there was anything to say. Hu begged the judge to judge according to fair law. Even if I die, I will not complain. If my crime is not deserved, then please release me on bail to avoid suffering more. (To be continued)

The Case of the Arrest of Demon Bandits in Jinan 68

Jinan Correspondence: Yesterday morning (the 4th), the Special Operations Team of the Public Security Bureau of the Provincial Capital of Jinan arrested the self-proclaimed Demon Bandit Pseudo-Emperor Li Lechuan, the Pseudo-Empress Song Wangshi, and the Pseudo-Earth Emperor Fu Baoqi at No. 124 Houyingfang. In addition, the carpenter Zhi Huaqing was arrested on Zhengjue Temple Street. More than 30 items such as imperial carriages, spirit tablets, and wooden oxen were found, along with three wooden boxes and one wicker package containing dragon robes and other imperial garments. The Public Security Bureau's Judicial Section conducted an interrogation that same evening and transferred them to the Provincial Government, where Chairman Han will review the case. Details are as follows:

The Pseudo-Emperor Li Lechuan is from Lucheng, 140 li southwest of Linyi County, and is 40 years old with no profession. Song Wangshi, the Pseudo-Empress, is 53 years old and from Anjiazhuang, Linyi County. She is Li's cousin (it is said that her husband, Song Qizeng, once served as the Prefect of Yangzhou and is skilled in incantations and spirit writing). The Pseudo-Earth Emperor Fu Baoqi is a tailor from Linyi who resides at No. 124 Houyingfang in this city. Recently, they had wild ideas and exploited the ignorance and corrupt thinking of the villagers to create rumors and incite people. They claimed to be acting under Heaven's mandate as the True Emperor. Song Wangshi also used witchcraft such as incantations and spirit writing to deceive the villagers, claiming that she was a disciple of a certain Buddha who had descended to earth to relieve suffering. Many ignorant women were deceived by her. Therefore, they carried out activities on a large scale. On the one hand, they contacted the Red Spear Society and others in various counties in southern Shandong to spread their influence. On the other hand, they secretly raised funds from various places in the name of offerings, and quite a few people were deceived. According to the donation records found, the amount of donations has reached millions. Li and others then secretly enjoyed the imperial system, establishing the pseudo-regime of "Later Qing". Li Lechuan called himself the "Emperor." The puppet organization of Manchuria also sent so-called "Imperial Envoys" to Linyi to secretly collude with him, attempting to disrupt Shandong. With external support, the Li bandits became even more active, appointing the Liu sisters, Fifth and Sixth, from the county as the Pseudo-East and West Palaces, and also assigning prime ministers and other pseudo-officials, planning to launch an uprising on the third day of the third month of next year. For a time, many ignorant villagers in various counties in southern Shandong were lured by them, and their potential power was quite significant. Later, Li Lechuan, fearing that the situation in Linyi was too sensitive and that there might be accidents, secretly traveled to Jinan with his cousin Song Wangshi (i.e., the Pseudo-Empress) in June and stayed at the home of the Pseudo-Earth Emperor Chen Baoqi at No. 124 Houyingfang, still secretly carrying out all activities. When the Provincial Government learned of this, it ordered Liu Yaoting, the captain of the Special Operations Team of the Public Security Bureau, to be responsible for the investigation. After receiving the order, Liu Yaoting sent many officers to secretly investigate. Because Li's organization was extremely strict, it took several months to fully understand everything. The Director of the Public Security Bureau, Wang Kairu, reported this, and at 7:00 am yesterday morning, Liu Yaoting personally led the police team to surround Fu Baoqi's residence in Houyingfang, arresting the Pseudo-Later Qing Emperor Li Lechuan, the Pseudo-Empress Song Wangshi, and the Pseudo-Earth Emperor Fu Baoqi on the spot. Another self-proclaimed "Human Emperor" escaped. In addition, the carpenter Zhi Huaqing and others (i.e., those who made the wooden oxen and other pseudo-artifacts) were arrested on Zhengjue Temple Street, totaling four people. Zhi is 36 years old and from Changqing. During the search of the Fu and Zhi residences, the so-called full set of ceremonial guard instruments was found, including door knives, elephant nose knives, longevity swords, sun, moon, stars, 　, fingers, hands, fists, palms, golden hooks, axes, Chao Tian Cheng, and more than 30 other items. There was also a spirit tablet building, with two dragons spitting whiskers and fully engraved with the character "王" (king) on yellow silk, and a wooden ox with four wheels, each embroidered with the character "王" (king) on its forehead and upper lip. In addition, there were three wooden boxes and one wicker package containing dragon robes, phoenix gold crowns, and other items. There were also many stationery items and a donation record book from various places. The Special Operations Team Captain Liu Yaoting took all the criminals and pseudo-artifacts to the Special Operations Team for interrogation. Li Lechuan and others confessed to all the above facts. They were then transferred to the Judicial Section of the Public Security Bureau at 8:00 pm and then transferred to the Provincial Government for Chairman Han to personally interrogate. However, several commissioners sent by the pseudo-organization and the Liu sisters of the Pseudo-East and West Palaces are still under investigation. According to reports, in the autumn of the 17th year, Ma Qiwei from Changqing County claimed to be the emperor and caused trouble in Zhoucun. After the army went to suppress and captured many people, Ma escaped. Now there is Li Lechuan, which can be said to be no coincidence. It can be seen that the minds of ordinary ignorant people are still anesthetized by the imperial system of thousands of years. This is also a hidden worry for the country and society. (December 5th)

Qingpu

Farmers' Bank Begins Pawning Rice 72

The Qingpu Branch of the Jiangsu Provincial Farmers' Bank had rice pawning facilities two years ago to help farmers. This year, Qing County has a bumper harvest of rice, and the price of rice has plummeted as a result, causing great losses to poor farmers. Moreover, it is currently the period for paying rent, and farmers are in urgent need of money. Therefore, the bank started pawning rice in Rihejiang on the 3rd of this month. It is reported that more than 250 shi were pawned on the first day.

Deputy Head of the Regiment Rapes a Woman from a Good Family 73

Cao, from Beizhen, Baihejiang, has a daughter who is hot-tempered and not unattractive. She married Yang from the same town. At first, the couple was quite harmonious. Since she became acquainted with Yang Hancha, who lives next door to Cao's family and serves as the deputy head of the town's security regiment, she suddenly became restless and secretly met with him under the guise of shopping. Her parents ordered her to return home, but she threatened to commit suicide. A month ago, her father died, and the two have been living together as a couple. However, Hancha's family is wealthy and happy, and his wife is ugly and very fierce. Knowing their secret, she hated them very much. One night this month, seeing her husband enter Cao's house, she waited outside the door for about two hours. When Cao's daughter came out, his wife stepped forward and caught the two of them. She fully intended to make a scene, but the two begged her in every way and promised not to do it again, so she let them go. Yang then submitted a petition requesting a divorce and compensation for the loss. After mediation by various parties, Hancha paid Yang more than 400 yuan as a marriage fee, and the matter was settled. However, after the divorce, Cao's daughter went to Hancha's house every day to make trouble, insisting on entering as a concubine. Because of his fierce wife, he dared not agree to her request and is currently arguing, unable to resolve the matter.

Italian Sericulture Expert Comes to Wuxi for Inspection 74

Italian sericulture expert Maria was dispatched by the Italian government to inspect the sericulture situation in China. She arrived in Nanjing a few days ago and visited Chen Gongbo, the Minister of Industry, to inquire about everything. Chen said that Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces are the main silk-producing areas in China, especially Wuxi, which is the most developed area. Therefore, he ordered He Yushu, the Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Industry, to accompany Maria to Wuxi for inspection. However, Director He accompanied the Director of the Ministry of Industry to Jurong Zhushui last Thursday to inspect mulberry and sericulture in preparation for planning a model mulberry and sericulture area. Upon hearing the news of Maria's arrival in Nanjing, he rushed back to receive her. Today, they came to Wuxi together. The silk factory industry in our city has already prepared to welcome them.

Court Accountant Accused of Being Escorted to Wuxi 75

Lei Renlong, the former president of the Wujin County Court, was accused of illegal malfeasance. The High Court dismissed him and sentenced him to one year of imprisonment and a fine of 600 yuan. However, Lei refused to accept the sentence and declared in court that he would appeal. Now, Lei's grandson, Shu De, said that Xu Yucheng, a Yixing native and the accountant during his grandfather's tenure, had forged a 500-yuan check to frame his grandfather. He then twisted Xu into the Wujin Public Security Bureau and transferred him to the County Court. On the one hand, Lei Shude filed a complaint with the High Court requesting a transfer of jurisdiction. The High Court designated the Wuxi County Court to hear the case. Yesterday, the Wujin County Court sent police to escort Xu to Wuxi. Prosecutor Shen opened a court to interrogate him and ordered Xu Yucheng to be detained pending investigation.

Five Rural Warehouses to be Established First 76

This year's autumn harvest is abundant, but the price of rice has fallen tragically, which has had a major impact on the rural economy in various places. The Jiangsu Provincial Jinghu Food Regulation Association has repeatedly held meetings and decided to set up public warehouses to handle agricultural loans. The Wuxi Farmers' Bank has actively carried out this plan within its fourth district. However, the construction of warehouses and the allocation of collateral are quite cautious. Recently, it has been decided to establish five locations first: 1. Dongting Town in the tenth district; 2. Anzhen in the eighth district; 3. Shitou Town in the fifth district; 4. Qianqiao Town in the fourth district; 5. Nanqiao Town in the third district. The above five locations started lending and accepting collateral yesterday. The collateral is stipulated to be rice, wheat, beans, and native cloth, mortgaged at 60% of the value of the goods, with a monthly interest rate of 1%, plus a storage fee. The term is temporarily set at one year. When mortgaging, the local township chief must provide proof and guarantee to ensure thoroughness. The protection problem will be handled by the police and business groups in each township.

Changshu

Manpower-Powered Rickshaws Resume Work Unconditionally 79

The manpower-powered rickshaw pullers in our city went on strike on the 1st of this month because they demanded that the owners reduce the rent of the rickshaws. Some of them were forced to resume work two days later but were stopped by the public. As a result, it has been four days since then. Some rickshaw pullers had no way to make a living and pawned their clothes and belongings, but it was still difficult to maintain themselves. They were in a dilemma. On the morning of the 5th, one or two people were forced by livelihood to try to pull rickshaws and no one stopped them. As a result, more and more people dragged rickshaws, and by 4:00 pm, no one stopped, and the entire group resumed work. Seeing this situation, the owners had pity on the workers and decided to convene a meeting of all the rickshaw owners on the afternoon of the 6th to discuss the reduction of rent.

Establishment of the Construction Bank Fund Confirmed 80

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction believes that the Provincial Construction Bank is the central institution for the province's construction funds, and its prosperity or decline is of great importance. Yesterday, it ordered the construction bureaus of various counties to allocate half of the construction funds collected by each county, totaling approximately 500,000 yuan, to the Construction Bank Fund so that it can be established as soon as possible for business. Blocking the River Dams Returning to the Yangtze River 81

Recently, the water level of the canal has been decreasing day by day, which has not only had a major impact on the irrigation of farmland, but also caused great difficulties for ordinary passengers due to the suspension of small steamboats. In addition, the lack of water in the rivers of various counties and cities north of the Yangtze River and the fire protection issues are of great concern. People from various counties have requested the Canal Engineering Bureau to quickly block all the canal dams returning to the Yangtze River in order to control the water flow and avoid excessive water leakage. It is reported that the bureau has begun to block the dams and can complete them all within a few days.

The total amount per mu is 4 jiao and 5 fen and 3 hao of silver yuan.

The Case of Abandoning a Body to Destroy Evidence Has Been Judged 86

In Hengjingqiao, the fifth district of Jiaxing,

the farmer Zhang Achang caught the unemployed worker Fu Zhaofu, who was stealing and attempting to rape. Fearing that he would make a scene, he stuffed cotton into his mouth, causing him to suffocate to death. He then threw the body into the river in an attempt to destroy evidence. Regulations for Autumn Harvest in Disaster Areas 88

Although there were many good harvests in the diked fields of various counties this year, there were also quite a few dry fields affected by drought. During the autumn, more than 20 counties reported disasters. The departments of civil affairs and finance commissioned surveys, but the affected counties still disputed the reported harvest numbers. After several deliberations, no decision was made. Subsequently, the departments of civil affairs and finance carefully discussed and stipulated the harvest numbers, which were telegraphed to the affected counties for announcement. The harvest numbers for each county are as follows: Tongcheng 80%, Wuwei 95%, Chaoxian 80%, He County 95%, Hanshan 80%, Guiyou 80%, Tongling 82%, Dongliu 85%, Dangtu 95%, Fanchang 90%, Fengyang 65%, Huaiyuan 76%, Shou County 65%, Dingyuan 70%, Fengtai 70%, Fuyang 70%, Yingshang 70%, Hao County 80%, Quanjiao 70%, Sixian 65%, Hongze 70%, Tianchang 75%.

Yesterday's Cable to the Third Plenary Session

With the Third Plenary Session scheduled to be held in mid-month, the Northeast Volunteer Army Transportation Corps specifically cabled all members of the session yesterday, requesting that they advocate for determined resistance against Japan in order to achieve the goal of recovering lost territory and expelling the violent Japanese from the country. The original cable reads: "To all members of the Third Plenary Session of Nanjing, all of you are aware of the rampant and escalating tyranny of Japanese imperialism, which is the result of our government's deliberate reliance on the League of Nations and lack of resolve to resist. Now, the weakness of the League of Nations' inability has been fully exposed; not only is it unable to sanction violent Japan, but it also seeks to place our Northeast territory under international co-management. Moreover, the treacherous schemes of imperialism in international affairs are emerging one after another, first by promoting a Japanese-Russian alliance to restrain the United States and France, and then by expanding military power to threaten the League of Nations. Amidst this treacherous international situation, our authorities, apart from sending two or three representatives to attend the League of Nations to engage in verbal battles, have made no other preparations. The dangers ahead are truly unbearable to mention. However, the reason why tens of counties in the Northeast have not yet changed color and the people have not become slaves of a conquered nation is due to the strength of the Northeast anti-Japanese armies. Now, the Northeast anti-Japanese armies are suffering from a lack of clothing, ammunition, and food, and are also under the general offensive of the Japanese army. The plenary session should seek to provide practical assistance to these patriotic men. The purpose of the team's organization is to provide practical assistance to the people. If the government is to recover the lost territory in the Northeast by force, it should rely on a massive armed force as the basis for recovering the lost territory in the Northeast. Rehe is the gateway to North China, a natural stronghold that has been repeatedly reported to be under strain since mid-July. For the sake of preserving North China and recovering the lost territory in the Northeast, the plenary session should urgently order the government to swiftly dispatch heavy troops to garrison in order to maintain the advantageous position of being able to defend and attack. The above-mentioned views are necessary conditions for determined resistance against Japan. Therefore, we cable requesting that you members deeply study this with the eye of a revolutionary, establish the greatest determination and conviction, advocate for determined resistance against Japan, and adopt thorough and appropriate methods to cope with the current crisis. The nation's survival depends on leading the people to fight against the violent Japanese. This telegram is sent for your consideration."

Police Obstruct Boy Scouts 99

Hindering the National Salvation Movement

A Thorough Investigation and Strict Punishment Should Be Requested

The New Sound Society reports that during the City Chamber of Commerce Boy Scout troop's charity performance to raise funds for Northeastern refugees, while selling tickets in the Baoshan Road area, police officer number 2729 from the 1st Section of the 5th District, obstructed them because he was unable to obtain free tickets. The society was extremely indignant upon hearing this and has sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau, requesting strict punishment for the officer as a warning to others. The letter states: "To the esteemed Public Security Bureau, in order to provide relief to Northeastern refugees who have taken up arms, our society has initiated a fundraising charity performance and, starting on the 1st of this month, instructed the Boy Scout troop to sell tickets door-to-door in order to raise substantial funds for relief efforts. We have previously submitted this to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for record and requested that your bureau instruct your subordinates to provide protection. Now, according to the ticket sales department, at 2 PM on the afternoon of the 4th, when the Boy Scouts went to the Baoshan Road area to sell tickets, a police officer number 2729 from the 1st Section of the 5th District came forward and forcibly demanded tickets. After the Boy Scouts politely explained that the tickets were all for donations to Northeastern refugees and could not be given away, the police officer left in a huff. The next day, the Boy Scouts returned to the same area to sell tickets, but the police officer obstructed them, spreading the word to various shops not to buy the tickets, and even took the Boy Scouts to the 1st Section of the 5th District, ordering them to stop selling tickets. Our society cannot bear the loss of our national territory, so we are speaking out for the Northeastern refugees who have taken up arms and initiating a charity performance. Any person with breath and blood who is not insane should strive to promote the spirit of national salvation and support this righteous cause. Although your bureau, constrained by regulations, cannot actively protect the Boy Scouts' ticket sales, it should certainly not prohibit or obstruct them. Whether or not to purchase tickets should be left to the conscience of the citizens. However, the police officer, harboring resentment for not obtaining free tickets, went so far as to obstruct this city-wide national salvation movement, acting in a contradictory and ignorant manner. Therefore, we specially request that your bureau swiftly conduct a thorough investigation and impose strict punishment as a warning to others. We eagerly await your response. Respectfully submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau."

Kim Cheol's Heartrending Conversation 100

Eternal Farewell to the Three Hans (Korea)

Afraid of Becoming a Double Colonial Slave

The New Sound Society reports that Kim Cheol and his son, naturalized Koreans who were arrested by the Japanese after they illegally entered the French Concession, have left Shanghai for elsewhere. Before leaving, Kim expressed his indignation to his friends. His lawyer, Wu Kaisheng, has decided on a course of action for negotiations, which are detailed below.

Kim Cheol was escorted out of Shanghai by his friends. The car was equipped with two self-defense guns in case of a Japanese attack, intending to fight to the death and perish together. One of his friends returned to Shanghai yesterday and told the reporter about Kim Cheol's conversation, which roughly stated: "I am a Korean who has been engaged in the restoration movement since the fall of my country. I have repeatedly failed, but this is not the first time. I always feel that China and Korea are brothers in history and interdependent in geography. If the younger brother dies, the elder brother will be defeated, like the loss of lips and the coldness of teeth. The Japanese want to destroy China, they must first destroy Korea. If Korea is destroyed, China will not be safe. Discerning people can see this. The Qing Dynasty figures like Zhang Peilun and Li Hongzhang all foresaw this, but unfortunately Empress Dowager Cixi did not use their strategies. If the Chinese people had aided the Korean restoration earlier, it would have been successful, and there would have been no incident in the Eastern Provinces. Because my patriotic work was difficult to produce results, I naturalized as a Chinese citizen in 1929, just like Li Ling said, 'Born as an extraordinary person, dying as a ghost in a foreign land,' bidding an eternal farewell to the Three Hans. Who would have thought that the Japanese would have the September 18th Incident last year and the January 28th Incident this year? I lament my misfortune, already a colonial slave of Korea, I will become a colonial slave of China. If China falls, the Chinese people will be a single colonial slave, while I will be a double colonial slave. What life experience could be more bitter than this?" At this point, his friend wept, and Kim also shed tears. He continued, "My anti-Japanese movement has a long history, and I am very familiar with many comrades in China and Korea. This time, being sold out was unexpected and was caused by my son Kim Cheol-nyeon being young, inexperienced, and overly enthusiastic. My acquaintance with Huang Zhanying was only last year. At that time, Huang was with Lawyer Wu Chengyu for a long time, and because I trusted Mr. Wu, I suffered this misfortune. Now I have suffered torture, but fortunately, I am still alive. This ambition will not change. My life was ended by the Japanese on the 30th of last month. The Kim Cheol from now on can be said to be a new life. Someone newly out of the gate is not afraid of death. I will tread on the bloodstains of the martyrs of China and Korea and move forward. I deeply hope to tell Chinese comrades to work together." The reporter visited Lawyer Wu Kaisheng, who is handling the case yesterday.

Lawyer Wu Kaisheng's Investigation

Lawyer Wu is paying close attention to this case and has decided on three measures: 1) Request the Municipal Government and the French Consul to negotiate with the Japanese Consul to prevent the Japanese from illegally arresting naturalized Chinese citizens in the French Concession in the future. 2) Request the French Consul to protect the safety of Chinese citizens and all naturalized foreigners in the French Concession, even if they commit criminal offenses, they must be dealt with according to legal procedures. 3) Demand a prompt response to Lawyer Cai's request for the return of Kim Cheol's belongings. He will do his utmost to achieve a satisfactory outcome to protect the safety of naturalized citizens.

Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund Loan for Road Construction 102

Material Purchases Must Be Reviewed by the Board of Directors

Equipment and Materials Must Be Stamped with the Society's Symbol

Personnel Must Be Sent to Participate in the Material Purchase Committee

The Central News Agency reports that the Board of Directors of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund has approved the Ministry of Railways' request for a loan, but the contract has not yet been signed. According to sources, during the meeting, the British Deputy Chairman, Mr. Massy, noted that the Huai River Conservancy Commission had previously borrowed funds from the fund for river management but had not yet repaid them. Therefore, he proposed that the Ministry of Railways' purchase of materials with this loan must be stamped with the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund symbol for identification and to clarify the debt. After discussion, it was resolved that in the future, the Ministry of Railways must submit detailed lists of materials purchased in Britain to the Board of Directors for review, and all equipment and materials must be stamped with the society's symbol next to the manufacturer's mark. Furthermore, the Board of Directors will send a representative to participate in the Material Purchase Committee. It is also reported that the loan contract stipulates that the Guangdong-Hankou Railway must be completed within three years.

Reporting on the War Situation and Requesting Relief

At this time of utter desperation, we have no choice but to ask our compatriots for help. We have long known that you gentlemen of your esteemed association have a long-standing love for the country and are generous in relieving suffering. At this time when 30 million people in the Northeast are in deep water and dire straits, and hundreds of thousands of territories have changed color, there must be sufficient relief. Therefore, we have specially sent Mr. Zhen Daitian, Chief of Staff of our unit, as a representative of all comrades in our unit, to go to Shanghai to plead for help from all walks of life. We still beg you to donate widely and collect small amounts to make a large sum. It is easy to hold up a crowd, and it is good to have more and more. Our unit vows to fight the Japanese bandits to the end, and even if there is only one soldier left, we will not be ashamed of being an ally under the city. We earnestly hope that our compatriots and gentlemen will consider the plight and lend a helping hand. The New Commander of the Japanese Navy's Third Fleet, Minei, Arrives in Shanghai 115

Landing This Morning

The new Commander of the Japanese Navy's Third Fleet stationed in Shanghai, Vice Admiral Minei, will arrive in Shanghai from Japan today to take office and unify the Japanese warships on the Yangtze River. The details are as follows:

Entering Port at 8 AM This Morning

Vice Admiral Minei Mitsumasa's flagship Izumo left Sasebo on the 5th and arrived at Wusong last night. The ship anchored at Songkou and is scheduled to sail into the Huangpu River to stop in front of the Yangshupu Huishan Wharf at 8 AM this morning. Upon hearing the news, Commander of the Japanese Naval Forces Sakano, Rear Admiral Sugisaka, Rear Admiral Tashiro, and Minister Arima Akira and Consul Ishi were all at the pier to welcome him. Sugisaka also sent 200 marines to protect the landing near the pier at that time.

Destroyers Arrive as Escort

The destroyers of the 27th Division, the Kure, Ashi, and Hishi, led by Lieutenant Colonel Fujita, first arrived in Shanghai and anchored in front of the Osaka Wharf in Yangshupu. Yesterday, Fujita visited Commander Sakano on the Ataka ship and paid respects to the Japanese Consul and the head of the civilian group in the afternoon. It is also heard that the fourth warship, the Hōshō, will arrive together with the flagship Izumo this morning.

Control of the Yangtze River Fleet

The warships directly under the command of the Third Fleet, as determined by the Japanese Navy Ministry and Minei, are the flagship Izumo, the cruiser Okinoshima, and four ships of the 27th Destroyer Division, totaling seven ships. The defense zone will be from Shanghai to Nanjing, while the 17 ships of the First Overseas Dispatch Force will be solely responsible for the inland defense zone of the Yangtze River, from Wuhu to Hankou and from Xiang to Changsha and Sichuan to Chongqing. The flagship will be designated as the Ataka and will be commanded by Sakano but also subject to Minei's command. When necessary, the 24 ships will be commanded by the Third Fleet, with Sakano as his deputy. Therefore, after Minei takes office, he will need to visit the capital and inspect the various ships on the Yangtze River.
