Inspection Record of the Completion of Dike Works by the National Government Flood Relief Association

Xujiawei Dike Works 118

The inspection schedule for December 2nd was as follows: At 9:30 AM, the Jiangxin steamer left Jiujiang upstream. At 11 AM, they took sampans to inspect the Xujiawei Dike Works on the south bank of Houjiawan, 20 li upstream from Jiujiang. At 12 PM, they returned to the main steamer for lunch. At 3 PM, they took sampans to inspect the north bank of the Yongquan Dike in Tianjiazhen, 3 kilometers away. At 4 PM, they returned to the main steamer and sailed directly to Hankou. The Xujiawei Dike Works, also under the jurisdiction of the Fifth District Engineering Bureau and contracted to the Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee, is only 200 steps from the riverbank, about 4 fen chi high, and 3 meters wide. The project appeared solid. The entire group briefly surveyed it, and returned to the main steamer at 11:30 AM. The steamer sailed at 12 PM. At 1:30 PM, they passed Wuxue without stopping. At 3 PM, they landed at Makou, Guangji County, to inspect the dike works contracted by the Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee to Wuxue. From Wuxue up to Hankou, it all belongs to the Fifth District Engineering Bureau, whose director, Yang Si-lian, is knowledgeable in hydraulic engineering.

Inspection of the Fifth District 119

The Fourth District Engineering area is in the Gan River and Poyang Lake area, with the bureau's office in Nanchang. It was originally planned to go to Nanchang from Jiujiang for inspection, but the plan was temporarily abandoned due to time constraints. From Wuxue upwards is the Fifth District Engineering area, from the south bank of the Yangtze River from Jinkou Town, Wuchang County, to Jianfeng Mountain, Yangxin County, and from Dajun Mountain, Hanyang County, to Wuxue Town, Guangji County, divided into ten sections. The total dike length is 363.7 kilometers. A total of 3,491,340 cubic meters of earthwork has been completed, with a total expenditure of 184,400 yuan for administrative expenses. The actual amount of wheat and grain distributed was 30,416.6 tons. The number of disaster workers was 133,200.

Jianghan Engineering Bureau 120

Regarding water conservancy projects, Hubei Province manages them relatively well along the Yangtze River, having considerable funds as a foundation, approximately 2 million yuan annually. Initially, the Hubei Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau was in overall charge, not under the jurisdiction of the Construction Department. Later, the Water Conservancy and Dike Works Bureaus were established separately, with the Dike Works Bureau holding the real economic power. At the same time, the Disaster Relief Committee established the Jianghan Engineering Bureau as the governing and post-disaster reconstruction organization for the completed dikes in the province. After Chairman Chiang's inspection of various water conservancy projects, he considered the work not entirely satisfactory and therefore abolished the Water Conservancy and Dike Works Bureaus, with the Jianghan Dike Works Bureau exclusively responsible for all water conservancy matters in the province. The takeover has recently been completed. It is heard that future plans will focus on: (1) Expediting the construction of various areas where construction was previously impossible due to the Communist bandit situation, aiming for complete completion within the shortest possible time; (2) Striving to devise dike protection strategies. According to engineering staff, Hubei's dike projects are the most perfect among all provinces because Hubei workers themselves have extremely rich experience in dike construction, which has invisibly created a foundation for superior results. Jiangsu and other provinces have always paid attention to river channels, and so on.

Perfect Dike Works 121

The perfection of Hubei's dike works is most immediately apparent to us in the Yongquan Dike within the Fifth District project. The Jiangxin steamer arrived at Makou, Guangji County at 3:30 PM, backed by mountains and facing water, a charming scene with a poetic feel. The entire group boarded sampans and crossed to the north bank, reaching the Yongquan Dike after a few hundred steps. The dike is 3 meters wide and approximately 9 kilometers long, starting from Wuxue in the east and ending at Qichun County in the west, rebuilt on the old dike. The five major breaches at the time have all been repaired, and the project is exceptionally solid. The lush grass along both sides provides protection. It is heard that Director Yang Si-lian of the Fifth District Engineering Bureau sowed Panicum repens seeds, which grew very quickly, resulting in today's achievements. The dike surface is extremely flat, without any unevenness. Mr. Li Zu-shen said that this is indeed an ideal dike. At 4:30 PM, they returned to the main steamer and continued upstream. At 5:30 PM, they arrived at Qipanzhou, Weiyuan Estuary, under the jurisdiction of Yangxin County, Hubei. The entire group again boarded small boats to inspect the Chenzhen Dike on the south bank, which is approximately 8.8 kilometers long and equally perfect as the Yongquan Dike. Both the Yongquan Dike and Chenzhen Dike face the river and are backed by mountains, both producing coal and other minerals. There are many coal kilns near the Yongquan Dike, specializing in the manufacture of coal balls, making a considerable profit. At 6 PM, they returned to the main steamer, which sailed directly to Hankou. After dinner, Executive Yuan Secretary-General Chu Min-yi gave a Tai Chi performance and showed flood relief films.

Harmony in Hankou 122

The Jiangxin steamer is expected to arrive in Hankou tomorrow morning (the 3rd), followed by a luncheon hosted by the Jianghan Engineering Bureau at noon, and a banquet hosted by the Hankou Municipal Government and various sectors in the evening. On the 4th, Chairman Chiang will host a banquet, starting at 5 PM, before inspecting dike works at Xinti, Jianli, Yuekou, and other places, including bandit areas, then return to Hankou and proceed north to Zhengzhou and Luoyang. (Sent by Qian Hua from Hankou on the morning of the 3rd) Telegram from the Dike Works Inspection Team: Song, Chairman of the National Government Flood Relief Committee, please note: This time, colleagues and others participated in the Dike Works Inspection Team, departing from Shanghai on the 11th and arriving in Beijing on the 20th to attend the Dike Works Completion Ceremony, then boarding the steamer. However, due to the excessive length of the dike lines in various districts along the way and the shortness of time, we could only selectively disembark to inspect them in sequence each day. On the 21st, from Zhenjiang to the Foganzhou Dike and Guadong Dike on the north bank of the First District; on the 22nd, from Wuhu to the Yijishan Dike and Lugang Dike on the south bank of the Second District, and in the afternoon to the Huangsitan Dike on the south bank of the Second District; on the morning of the 30th, to the Liubai Zhang Dike in Tongcheng County on the north bank of the Second District. The dike was not initially included in the discussion due to the Engineering Bureau and construction was delayed, with about one-tenth of the project still unfinished and currently under construction. In the afternoon, we continued to inspect the Guangjiwei Dike of the Third District in Huaining County; on the morning of December 1st, to the Mahua Dike in Wangjiang County, Anhui Province, of the Third District; in the afternoon, to the Huikou Dike of Jiujiang County and the Duanyao Dike of Huangmei County, both on the north bank, repaired on behalf of the Chinese and Foreign Famine Relief Committee. In summary, in the past few days, we have inspected various dikes and referred to the Engineering Bureau's various district engineering overviews and standard drawings to separately inspect the dike surface width and the internal and external slopes, all of which still meet the requirements. The height of each dike exceeds last year's flood level by one meter. We have secretly investigated that your association, after the disaster last year, carefully planned and maintained the project, completing this great project in a few months with the most economical plan. After our inspection, we deeply admire it. This year's autumn harvest is abundant, and the residents along the river especially appreciate the great virtue. In addition to continuing the inspection according to the itinerary and reporting at any time, we know that you are concerned, and we respectfully submit this telegram for your perusal. Dike Works Inspection Team: Xu Shi-ying, Wen Lan-ting, Simpson, Li Zu-shen, Zhou Xiang-xian, Xi De-jiong, etc., and all colleagues kowtow.

Water and Electricity Questions in the Chinese and Foreign Concessions>

Telephone Contract 123

Regarding the issue of negotiating a contract for installing telephones in areas with roads built beyond the concessions, according to Xu Yuan-fang, Secretary of the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, everything is now complete for the contract. However, Director Huang believes that a Chinese version of the contract must be used for signing, so the concession telephone company still needs to hire lawyers to carefully discuss and translate the Chinese version into English before signing.

Electricity in West Shanghai 124

Regarding the issue of supplying water and electricity to areas with roads built beyond the concessions in West Shanghai, yesterday, Xu Yuan-fang, Secretary of the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, told the Central News Agency reporter that the water and electricity required by residents on both sides of the roads built beyond the concessions in West Shanghai could have been supplied by the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company or the Shanghai South China Merchants Electric Company. However, because the roads in the area were previously built by the concessions and it was inconvenient for the Chinese-run water and electricity companies to lay electrical conduits under the road surface, the Shanghai Electric Power Company of the concession has been supplying it. However, residents must first submit an application to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau for approval before sending it to the Electric Power Company for connection. In recent years, the number of residents on both sides of the roads built beyond the concessions has increased daily, and the demand for electricity has also increased. The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau has fixed regulations on the size of the electrical conduits, so the Shanghai Electric Power Company requested the Shanghai Municipal Government to replace the larger electrical conduits to supply larger power. The Municipal Government believes that this matter still needs to be discussed and appointed Huang Bo-qiao, Director of the Public Utilities Bureau, Cai Zeng-ji, Director of the Finance Bureau, and Xu Pei-huang, a Municipal Government Specialist, to represent the Municipal Government and contact the company to discuss this matter. The initiative actually started during the tenure of former Mayor Zhang Qun and has been more than a year. Recently, the Shanghai Electric Power Company has again requested the Municipal Government to approve this request as soon as possible, so the Municipal Government ordered Director Huang and others to convene a meeting as soon as possible to decide whether to approve the request.

Radio Broadcasting 125

The Da Mei Evening News reports that the officers of the Chinese Broadcasting Association and the Wireless Radio Merchant Association of this port held an informal meeting with representatives of the Municipal Government and the two concession authorities at the Huangma Hang Hotel this afternoon (the 6th) to discuss methods for managing radio broadcasting in this port. Representatives of the Municipal Government and the two concession authorities attended the meeting as informal observers so that they could listen to the suggestions and opinions of the radio industry in order to negotiate a concrete management plan. In the future, after this plan is approved by all relevant organizations, the Municipal Government and the two concession authorities will make it into a law.

Yesterday's News of a Major Case of Fraudulent Relief: Suspension of Relief Funds in Wuhe County 127

Representatives of Wuhe County Arrived to Appeal

Quan Shao-wu Firmly Denied Suspension of Relief

Yang Shu-cheng, Quan Shao-wu, Wang Fan-wu, and Cha Liang-zhao, officials of the National Government Flood Relief Committee, were accused of embezzling relief grain and diverting relief funds from Anhui disaster relief matters for personal gain. The Standing Committee of the Anhui Native Place Association in Shanghai, including Li Zhen-ya, filed a lawsuit with the First Special District Local Court, which has been heard several times. All accusations against the first defendant, Yang Shu-cheng, have been heard. The previous hearing on the accusation against the second defendant, Quan Shao-wu, regarding the suspension of urgent relief funds to Wuhe County, was not yet completed. Yesterday afternoon, Presiding Judge Wu Ting-qi specially opened the Second Criminal Court to summon both parties and witnesses for continued examination. Many people were still crowding the court to listen. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that regarding the suspension of urgent relief funds to Wuhe, the Wuhe County Chamber of Commerce, Farmers Association, Education Association, and other legal entities had elected Chen Lu-zhen, the former chairman of the Wuhe County Relief Branch, to bring all relevant documents to the court for detailed verification. Chen Lu-zhen then explained the reason for Quan Shao-wu's suspension of urgent relief, stating that on May 21st of this year, two investigation committee members, He Bing-heng, who were sent to Wuhe by Commissioner Quan to investigate relief distribution, had a conflict with the local people. Commissioner Quan then telegraphed He and others to suspend relief until June 9th. Only after repeated appeals from local government agencies and groups did they continue to distribute relief, totaling a 15-day suspension. The relief distributed at that time was urgent relief. Judge Wu then examined the stub of the relief ticket issued by Quan Shao-wu on May 29th, which was presented previously. After Chen Lu-zhen carefully examined it, he added that this kind of stub had neither the seal of the National Government Flood Relief Committee nor the seal of the local county government. Moreover, if they had gone to distribute relief, there would be no receipt issued by the local relief branch for collecting funds. Therefore, not only was no relief distributed on May 29th, but the stub was probably forged and should be noted. The court then questioned the source of the stub presented by the defendant, Quan Shao-wu. Quan claimed that it was obtained from the director of the Bengbu Relief Audit Office. Quan also explained the reason why this ticket stub was different from other ticket stubs, saying that the relief authorities disliked the slow progress of relief in northern Anhui, so Xin Bosen of the Flood Relief Committee ordered him to form a joint committee in Bengbu to handle relief in northern Anhui in order to speed up the process. The Flood Relief Committee approved the on-site printing of relief tickets if they were insufficient. The stub presented was printed in Bengbu, so there was no seal of the National Government Flood Relief Committee. The relief funds were distributed by the joint committee. Therefore, the people of Wuhe opposed the joint committee and claimed that he had suspended relief because the relief funds were not distributed by the local flood relief association. The plaintiff's lawyer then presented the draft copies of various documents and telegrams related to the request for relief, stating that the court would understand that the suspension of relief was indeed the truth after reviewing the case file. Judge Wu then asked Chen Lu-zhen about the form of the relief ticket on June 9th. Chen replied that it also had no seal of the Flood Relief Committee or the county government. The court then instructed him: "You claim that the relief ticket stub on May 29th was forged because it did not have the seal of the National Government Flood Relief Committee. Why do you not question the ticket stub without a seal on June 9th?" He then turned to Quan Shao-wu and said that various documents and telegrams from the Anhui Provincial Government, the Anhui Provincial People's Hall, Wuhe County, and the workgroup of the National Government Flood Relief Committee all mentioned the suspension of relief, so the suspension of relief in Wuhe was indeed the case. However, the defendant, Quan Shao-wu, firmly denied it, saying that although there was a telegram sent to Wuhe after the conflict with the word "temporary suspension" in it, no relief was actually suspended. The words "suspension of relief" in the various documents and telegrams all originated from the word "temporary suspension." If the court considered the word "temporary suspension" to be a crime, the defendant would naturally accept it. However, if the fault of actually suspending relief was established, then he could not but defend himself. The plaintiff claimed that he suspended relief based on many empty words, but he had presented the relief ticket to prove that relief was still being distributed on May 29th, and the relief ticket stub on May 29th could also be obtained from Bengbu. Judge Wu adjourned the hearing because it was already dark and instructed that the hearing would continue on the afternoon of the 13th of this month.

Bloodshed Due to Banter 128

Diligence Has Merit ... Teasing is Useless

Zhang Ming-jin, an Anhui laborer working at the Texaco Wharf in Gaoqiao, Pudong, lived in the Xiao Sha-yun barbershop in that area. Zhang was fond of joking, which led to teasing and then to a serious argument with his colleague Wang Ming-biao. The two immediately fought on the wharf. Zhang Kong-wu was strong, and Wang could not win. Wang harbored resentment and gathered several people the day before yesterday afternoon to seek out Zhang for a fight in the barbershop, destroying the barbershop. Zhang, outnumbered, was stabbed in the head five or six times, bleeding profusely and falling unconscious. The barbershop owner, Chen Yun-you, returned home and saw the situation. After asking the reason, he reported it to the Fourth Police Station of the Third District. The police arrested Wang. Yesterday, he was transferred to the local court for examination.

A Rickshaw Puller Calculates Accounts with His Master

Shortly After Being Released from Prison, He Dared to Gather Gangsters to Extort Money, First Demanding 5,000 Yuan, Then Reducing it to 3,000 Yuan 129

| After Investigation, He was Sentenced to One Year in Prison |

Wang Ren-fu, the owner of Fenghe Paint Shop at No. 134 Shandong Road, lived at No. 1451 Zhonghua Road in the city. His son, Rui-bao, had been riding a reserved rickshaw pulled by Cai A-fu, a man from Tongzhou, to a school in the French Concession since April 27th of last year. While passing the Siming Guild Hall on Minguo Road, several kidnappers suddenly kidnapped Rui-bao, and Wang redeemed him with a huge sum of money. The Municipal Public Security Bureau arrested several kidnappers, who confessed that Cai A-fu was the mastermind. The Public Security Bureau arrested Cai, who frankly admitted to being an informant. He was sent to the Shanghai Local Court, which sentenced Cai to 12 years in prison. Cai appealed to the Suzhou High Court, which recently acquitted him and released him from prison on the 25th of last month. The day before yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, Wang Ren-fu was at Fenghe for business when Cai suddenly gathered several gangsters and came to Wang, saying, "I was arrested and sentenced to 12 years in prison because you reported me. I have been released from prison and came to settle the score for the losses I suffered. Quickly give me 5,000 gold yuan as compensation, or you should be careful when you go out, or I may have to kidnap your son again." He then reduced the amount to 2,000 yuan. Wang pretended to agree and promised to pay the money, but said he needed to go out to prepare it. Cai did not suspect and agreed. Wang then went out and reported to the General Inspection Office of the General Police Station. Chief Inspector Lu Lian-kui ordered detectives Liu Shao-kui, Gai Zhao-bin, and others to rush to the scene and arrest Cai and bring him back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Special Court's Criminal Division. The police lawyer Ru Bao-yi stated the case and said that he was now prosecuting according to Article 370, Section 3 of the Criminal Code, for attempted extortion. Wang Ren-fu and his bodyguard Chen Xiang-tao then filed a case to prove how the defendant had threatened him at the time. Cai A-fu confessed that Wang Ren-fu owed him 14 days of wages, so he went to settle the account and did not intend to extort money. He asked for leniency. Presiding Judge Feng Shi-de, after verifying the confession, announced the sentence in court: Cai A-fu was sentenced to one year of imprisonment for the crime of attempted extortion.

Case of Two Koreans Kicking a Chinese Man to Death 130

Final Appraisal Report Published

Confirmed that the Chinese Man was Kicked to Death by Koreans

Koreans Li Chang-lian and Gui Xi-ren had a dispute with an old woman from Changshu, Yao Chen, over the purchase of baked sweet potatoes, and kicked her second son, Yao Xiao-ji, in the abdomen, causing him to die after ineffective medical treatment. The local court appointed Prosecutor Yang Qi to conduct an interrogation together with Ma Zu-fan of the Investigation Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and Dr. Tenggong, appointed by the Japanese Consulate. They conducted a joint examination, but the Japanese doctor refused to conduct a joint examination because Yao Xiao-ji's abdomen had already been dissected before his death and it was impossible to determine who caused the fatal injury. Prosecutor Yang ordered the forensic doctor to conduct a forensic examination as required, which found that Yao Xiao-ji was indeed kicked in the abdomen, resulting in death. However, the Japanese Consulate considered the examination results questionable and did not allow the two Koreans to be punished. Therefore, Lou Ying, the Chief Prosecutor of the Local Court, sent a letter to the Zhenru Forensic Research Institute for a detailed autopsy. The autopsy was conducted on November 23rd, and a pathological tissue examination was performed. The appraisal report was prepared and sent to the court and the Municipal Public Security Bureau a few days ago, requesting them to negotiate with the Japanese Consulate. The conclusion of the appraisal report is recorded as follows: "Combining the above examination descriptions and the first to fifth appraisal items, a conclusion can be obtained, namely that Gui Xi-ren and Yao Xiao-ji fought with each other, and Gui Xi-ren used his foot to forcefully kick Yao Xiao-ji's abdomen, hitting the center of the navel (slightly to the left), causing a contusion of the abdominal wall. The force reached the deep part, causing a contusion and laceration of the jejunum wall in the abdominal cavity. Although the bleeding was stopped by surgery in the hospital, the intestinal contents leaked into the peritoneum, causing purulent acute peritonitis, resulting in death after five days of ineffective medical treatment." It is heard that Director Wen approved the letter and sent Jin Gong, the Director of the Fifth District, to the Japanese Consulate General's Office for serious negotiations.

Review of Opera Records 131

The Municipal Government Revised and Promulgated the Regulations Yesterday

Yesterday, the Municipal Government promulgated the revised regulations of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau for reviewing opera records. The original text is extracted below: Article 1: These regulations are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 12 of the Shanghai Municipal Public Entertainment Venue Management Regulations. Article 2: All performances of operas, songs, variety shows, and other operas in this city, or the production and sale of records (hereinafter referred to as "operas or records"), must apply to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau (hereinafter referred to as "the Bureau") for review in accordance with the provisions of these regulations. Article 3: When designing, arranging, or recording operas or records, the producer (if it is a legal person, the name and location of the office and the name and address of its representative should be stated) should submit an application form in advance and submit two copies of a concise description of the content of the opera or record, or the original script and the list of performers, for review by the Bureau. After approval, the performance or recording can be arranged. Article 4: Operas that have been approved for performance and records that have been recorded should be re-examined by the producer or holder before the public performance or sale by submitting two copies of the application form to the Bureau. However, operas performed and records recorded before the promulgation and implementation of these regulations should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 3. Article 5: For operas or records that have been approved for review, the Bureau will issue a license to allow public performance or sale. Article 6: If the content of an opera or record has any of the following circumstances, it may be rewarded: (a) Promoting patriotic thought and arousing national spirit; (b) Promoting inherent morality and benefiting social customs; (c) Excellent and noble performance art. Article 7: If the content of an opera or record has any of the following circumstances, it should be prohibited or revised: (a) Violating party principles and damaging the national system; (b) Obstructing public order and morals; (c) Promoting superstition, heresy, and feudal ideology. Operas or records that should be revised must be re-examined by the Bureau after revision. Article 8: If there is any change in the content of an opera or record that has been approved and licensed, the Bureau should be applied to for review again. Article 9: If an opera or record that has been approved and licensed is found to be inconsistent with the reviewer, its license may be revoked immediately, and its public performance or sale may be prohibited. Article 10: The review of operas or records shall be handled by the Opera Record Review Committee organized by 10 to 15 staff members designated by the Bureau. Members of the Review Committee may hold review certificates to inspect various public entertainment venues and record companies at any time. Article 11: These regulations may be revised at any time if there are any matters not covered. Article 12: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of submission to the Municipal Government for approval.

Local News: Yesterday's Cold Snap 132

The weather in Shanghai has been very warm recently, with temperatures often between 60 and 80 degrees. However, since the day before yesterday, it suddenly turned cold, and yesterday was even worse. The northwest wind howled relentlessly, and the temperature plummeted to below 40 degrees, a drop of about 30 degrees compared to the previous few days, presenting a harsh, cold scene.

An Elderly Woman, Anxious to Put Out a Fire, Forgets Her Grandson, Resulting in His Death 133

A Seven-Year-Old Child Tragically Burned to Death

Yesterday morning around nine o'clock, an elderly woman surnamed Zhang, who rented a room on the second floor of the Wan Chang Soy Sauce Garden at 1115-1117 Xin Zha Road, carelessly overturned a kerosene stove while cooking, causing an immediate fire. Employees of the garden noticed and called the fire department. By the time the fire trucks arrived, the fire had already broken through the roof. The woman was still trying to extinguish the fire, and her entire body was engulfed in flames. Firefighters used a ladder to pull her out of a window, but her limbs were already badly burned. She was rushed to Tongren Hospital for treatment. The fire was extinguished around 9:30 AM, having only destroyed one room on the mezzanine. After the fire was put out, firefighters investigating the cause of the fire suddenly discovered the charred body of a young child. Upon investigation, it was learned that the woman had a grandson named A Gen, only seven years old. In the chaos of the fire, the woman had been too focused on putting out the blaze and had forgotten to rescue the child, resulting in his tragic death.

Wang Xiaolai Discusses Family Education and Discipline 135

When he returns home, all of his children are as quiet as crows and sparrows, not daring to make a sound. They line up in the courtyard and are asked about their studies and character. Even those still in their mother's arms seem to want to stop nursing and stand up straight. As a result, although he has many children – twenty-five – the atmosphere in his home is extremely quiet, and nothing has ever been broken. This shows the importance of family education, and the Da Dong Bookstore's raising of capital for family education is an important undertaking. One Man Acts, One Man Pays: Murderer Drinks and Smokes After the Crime 136

Why Did Wang Ziqiang Mock Li Buyun? Two Apprentices Thus Became Bitter Enemies.

What Glory or Shame Does a Father's Employment Bring to His Son?

The Courage of Youth... Why Hold a Grudge and Kill?

Yesterday morning at midnight, a bloody incident occurred inside the Wanyuan Shun Kaoliang Wine Shop at 174 Datong Road, under the jurisdiction of the Fourth District of Zhabei. The parties involved were apprentices and fellow workers in the shop, and they were also from the same hometown. The details of the investigation are as follows.

What Does a Father's Lowly Position Have To Do With His Son? 137

Wang Lizhen, from Tongxiang, Zhejiang, works as an accountant in the Baoshan County Salt Guildhall at the intersection of Yongxing Road and Datong Road. His son, Wang Ziqiang, 17, was introduced by his uncle to work as an apprentice at the Wanyuan Shun Wine Shop at 174 Datong Road two years ago. Li Buyun, also from Tongxiang, works as a runner in the Songjiang County Salt Guildhall. Because he and Wang Lizhen live near each other in their hometown, they are very familiar with each other. Li's son, Li Yuanjing, 19, joined the shop as an apprentice five years ago. He has now completed his apprenticeship and been promoted to a fellow worker, earning a monthly salary of five yuan. He is quiet, studious, and often studies in his spare time. Wang Ziqiang, on the other hand, is arrogant and often boasts about his family background to his peers. He also mocks Yuanzhang and insults his father for his low position. As a result, Li feels resentful and has clashed with Wang repeatedly. But Wang does not restrain himself and continues to provoke Li, who cannot suppress his anger. Thus, the seeds of this incident were sown.

Murder in the Middle of the Night, Loud Cries for Help 138

Recently, the relationship between Wang and Li has deteriorated. Li has been harboring vengeful intentions, but Wang has not noticed. Around midnight yesterday morning, Li saw that the other workers were asleep. He put on his clothes, quietly left the bedroom on the upper floor of the shop's reception room, and walked slowly downstairs. He first went to the kitchen, found a cleaver, and then entered the shop's back room, where Ziqiang was sleeping. He held the knife and slashed at Ziqiang's head. Wang was startled by the pain and struggled violently, and his arms and legs were also cut. He cried out loudly for help. The people in the shop, alerted by the commotion, gathered around and saw Ziqiang lying motionless in a pool of blood, Yuanzhang standing blankly beside him, holding a cleaver. The crowd snatched the cleaver from his hand and asked Li why he had committed such a cruel act. Li replied, "One man acts, one man pays. I will not implicate you." With that, he pushed through the crowd, walked to the door of the shop, poured a bowl of wine from the wine jar, and took out something from his pocket and swallowed it with the wine. Seeing this, the crowd knew that he had taken poison and rushed forward to hold down his hands. They saw that Li still had half a piece of opium in his hand and quickly snatched it away and forced him to sit on a stool.

Twelve Cuts... Life is in Danger 139

The shop's other workers were terrified and quickly sent someone to report to the shop owner and Wang Lizhen. They also hired a car to take Li to Baolong Hospital and called the hospital, asking them to send an ambulance to take Wang Ziqiang away. They also reported the incident to the Fourth District Police Station. Yesterday afternoon, Li's father was also notified by the shop and rushed from Songjiang. However, Li Yuanzhang had not taken a deep dose of poison, so he was saved by the doctors at Baolong Hospital. The hospital then notified the Xin Zha Police Station, which sent detectives to arrest Li and interrogate him. The police ordered him to be detained. This morning, he was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, the police lawyer, explained the situation, saying that Wang Ziqiang's father had reported the incident to the Fourth District Public Security Bureau after his son was injured, but the Public Security Bureau had not sent anyone to the court today. He requested that the case be investigated. Judge Wu Zhen ordered Li Yuanzhang to be detained pending the Public Security Bureau's official transfer of the case. It was learned that Li had inflicted twelve cuts on Wang, four of which were to the head and were considered fatal, so his life was in great danger. Li's father visited Ziqiang in the hospital yesterday afternoon.

Taxpayers' Association Repeatedly Sends Letters to the Public Works Department, Requesting That It Order the Water Company Not to Cut Off Water 141

Water Fee Disputes Can Be Discussed at Length

Direct Action Endangers Residents' Lives

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association sent letters yesterday to the Public Works Department and its Director-General, stating: (1) "We are writing to inform you that according to a letter from the Deli Landlord Accounting Office, since the Shanghai Waterworks Company increased water rates, our company has been unable to pay due to the excessive burden. We believed that the dispute could be resolved through negotiations between your association, the water company, and the Public Works Department. However, the water company has taken high-handed measures, disregarding everything and abruptly cutting off the water supply to the Baifu and Bailu residential areas on Yangzhou Road, Fenzhou Road, and Huasheng Road at 11:00 AM this morning, causing immediate chaos. Hundreds of households in these two areas face the threat of being unable to cook, which is a major issue affecting social order and residents' lives. We are compelled to request that your association negotiate with the water company as soon as possible and insist that the water supply be restored before any further discussion can take place." The letter goes on to say that cutting off the water supply is not a viable solution to the water fee dispute. If those who depend on water as their lifeline were to take direct action similar to the water company's, the serious consequences would be easily imagined by your Director-General. We are sending this letter to request that you investigate the matter and promptly order the water company to restore the water supply in order to find a solution that benefits all parties. (2) "We are writing to inform you that according to a letter from the Fenxing Real Estate Company, our company has a block water agreement for its rental properties located on Zhejiang Road, Ningbo Road, Niuzhuang Road, and Weishui Lane. The water users are the tenants, and our company does not wish to continue its obligation to collect water fees on behalf of the Shanghai Waterworks Company. We have requested that water meters be installed in each household so that the company can directly collect water fees from the tenants, which is a reasonable request supported by the precedent of the electricity and telephone companies. However, in June of this year, the company unilaterally installed a master water meter and forced us to pay water fees. Our company cannot agree to this. However, as the meter was not installed in each household, we continue to pay water fees under the block water agreement and hold the funds in escrow pending resolution. We notified the water company of this matter in a letter dated October 24th, forwarded by the Real Estate Association. We have since received a letter from the company dated November 3rd, giving us until the 7th of this month to pay the water fees under the master water meter system, threatening to cut off the water supply. Such oppressive behavior affects the lives of our tenants, and as landlords, we cannot remain silent. We request that your association uphold justice and achieve a truly fair outcome, which would be fortunate for the tenants and the entire city. Furthermore, the company's master water meter system is one that our company has repeatedly stated that we object to, yet we have received bills from June to November totaling $2,190.32. The water fees for the Sanyou Society on the third floor of the building along the street are included in this amount, yet the company has also collected block water fees of 120 taels of silver for the months of June, July, August, and September. This demonstrates the company's self-contradictory and greedy behavior. Can a public utility as large as the Public Works Department act in such a way?" The letter goes on to say that until a reasonable solution can be found that is acceptable to all parties, it seems best to maintain the status quo. Adopting the method of cutting off the water supply to achieve a unilateral benefit is akin to blaming the fishpond for the fire at the city gate because one acknowledges that the water cannot be used to establish that the landlord is not acknowledging the master watermeter system. Since the tenants can prove that the increased rate would ultimately be their burden, the difficulties with cutting off the water supply may come from those outside the matter of tenants and landlords. Therefore, the Bureau should give the matter special attention. The letter also requested that the bureau follow the latest suggestions of the Association, and seek out the appropriate resolution.

National Crisis New Year Cards Welcome Imprints. Rixin Yudi Publishing House, located at No. 19 Baojiang Lane, Avenue Albert, is producing a type of national crisis New Year card. The back of the postcard features a map of the three northeastern provinces, containing over 200 place names and using various symbols to show the recent battle situation between the volunteer army and the enemy army. Areas held by our army that have not been lost are marked. Imprints are 1.6 yuan per hundred, with an additional 13 cents for postage outside the city. Those who wish to imprint their names and addresses can contact the publishing house.

Jixiang Bookstore Rents Novels. The Jixiang Bookstore on Luxiangyuan Road, Jiumu area, in the Chinese district of Shanghai, has created a novel rental department to reduce the burden on readers and provide convenience, renting out all kinds of famous and valuable novels. Recently, readers have been flocking to rent novels, which is a great event in the reading world. The rules are as follows: (1) The annual rental fee is 2.5 yuan, and the half-year rental fee is 1.8 yuan. (2) The deposit is 50% of the book's price. (3) Comic books cost 120 cash per book and require a deposit of 6 dimes. It is also reported that the bureau is widely collecting old Chinese and Western books.

Medical and Pharmaceutical Industry 151

Cihang Midwifery School Approved for Establishment. Dr. Wang Haoran, a famous doctor in Shanghai, invested in and established the Cihang Midwifery School in the 19th year of the Republic. He hired Chu Minyi, Wang Qizhang, Liu Zhigang, Zheng Shenchu, and others as school directors. After it opened, Dr. Wang sold his personal property for more than 20,000 yuan to provide the school's funds. Since then, the school's facilities have become increasingly perfect and the number of students has gradually grown. This summer, the Municipal Education Bureau set a deadline for private schools to apply for establishment, but the school still lacked funds. Dr. Wang generously planned to raise tens of thousands of yuan to be used as a fund for the establishment procedure, which was approved by the Municipal Education Bureau's meeting. The school's foundation is becoming more solid, and it is reported that a new plan will be implemented next semester, adding equipment, hiring famous doctors as professors, and expanding the number of students to popularize midwifery education.

Zibu Yanzegao. Jiang Yanzeshi's old shop outside of Shanghai's Xiaonanmen has a long-standing reputation. In addition to specializing in various famous plasters, pills, and powders, a new tonic medicine called "Zibu Yanzegao" has been newly developed. This medicine uses precious royal tonic ingredients and is effective for nourishing qi and blood, strengthening the essence, calming the nerves, promoting fluid production, and promoting blood circulation. It is mild in nature and has no drawbacks. It can be taken for weakness of qi and blood, fatigue, cough, seminal emission, insomnia, irregular menstruation in women, and malnutrition and weight loss in children, and has remarkable effects. It is indeed a wonderful product for winter conditioning. The price is 35 cents per ounce.

Reader's Advisor

㈠ Discussion of Questions Raised by Ms. Zhang Yunqiu 152

丨 See This Column on December 3rd

Mr. Lü Yuru reports: ㈠ "Things at their extreme will revert," and "Too much honey is not sweet." Excessive emotion inevitably leads to temporary rifts. Relationships formed from the illusion of love are even more certain to drop from boiling point to zero. ㈡ Those who have not yet married should carefully examine their partners. Those who are married should respect each other, be sincere and trustworthy, love without being disrespectful, and respect without fear, so that they can always get along harmoniously.

Mr. Mai Zifen reports: ㈠ This is due to the physics of "things at their extreme will revert" and the psychology of "marriage is the grave of love." ㈡ Before marriage, the heat of love should be controlled to prevent it from reaching boiling point. After marriage, efforts should be made to maintain the original love, such as occasional separations or traveling together.

Mr. Zhu Shaowen reports: ㈠ It is the result of the development of human laziness and greed. ㈡ The concepts of loyalty and forgiveness must be used to remedy it.

Mr. Zhou Guohua reports: ㈠ It is because one of the elements constituting "love" is missing between the spirit and the flesh. ㈡ (A) Mutual respect, love, and trust, (B) Ensuring financial affluence, (C) Being able to share both joys and sorrows, (D) Exercising self-restraint with reason, (E) Sleeping separately, (F) Having lively children.

Mr. Jing Zhen reports: ㈠ Due to misunderstanding of freedom or oppression from old-fashioned families. ㈡ From the government down to judicial officials, school teachers, and family elders, young people should be taught the true meaning of mutual understanding and assistance between husband and wife, sharing both joys and sorrows. Mr. Yan Yun reports: ㈠ It originates from the economic phenomena caused by the exploitative society; this is just a small branch of the entire social problem. ㈡ The social system must be thoroughly reformed. All idealistic methods are useless. Mr. Xie Xinwu reports: ㈠ (A) Before marriage, both sides conceal their weaknesses. After marriage, all weaknesses are exposed. (B) Life after marriage is very different from the ideals before marriage. ㈡ Mutual understanding, comparing other couples (less fortunate than oneself), extracurricular activities, and couple pastimes should be academic to make life less ordinary. Mr. Zhang Shaoliang reports: ㈠ Either due to economic pressure or a lack of personality in one party. ㈡ One must live within one's means and pay attention to personality cultivation.

Mr. Jin Mingchang reports: ㈠ Due to too much freedom before marriage and too little freedom after marriage, and neither party has fully examined the other before marriage. ㈡ The time between dating and engagement should be long. Both parties must be open and honest, understand and help each other, or go on outings and trips.

㈡ Suggestions for This Column 153

Mr. Ge Chuan-gui reports: 1. Your newspaper says "All problems and difficulties are not individual." I think you can only say "not all are individual," but you cannot say "none are individual." Moreover, those problems and difficulties that are "not individual" are certainly important, but those that are "individual" are particularly important to the person who raises the problem or difficulty. The "Reader Consultant" should also answer them. For example, regarding natural science mentioned in the "Concise Rules," if someone raises a question or doubt about chemistry or physics, it may not be something that the average reader wants to know, but the person who asks the question attaches great importance to it. 2. Since your newspaper has hired several experts, it seems that their names should be published, or at least it should be stated under each answer which expert answered it. This seems more solemn, and readers would seem happier because each expert is responsible for the answer. 3. Mr. Liu said, "Not to degenerate into the kind of three hundred solutions to arithmetic problems." Of course, that arithmetic expert does not have so much time to answer three hundred difficult problems for one reader, but I think if someone asks for a solution to an arithmetic problem, that arithmetic expert should be responsible for solving it for him. I think answering "special problems" for readers (e.g., how to solve a certain arithmetic problem, or what is the factual situation of a certain event in a certain country at a certain time) is more important and more difficult than answering many general questions (e.g., how to study or how to serve society). Fortunately, since there are experts, it is easy as long as each specializes in his own specialty. 4. Your newspaper advocates submitting more important issues to the public for discussion, and then your newspaper will synthesize opinions and make a conclusion. I think there are many issues that are not "opinions" issues. For example, arithmetic problems should always be studied by the arithmetic expert first. If he cannot figure it out, then it should be published in the newspaper and ask arithmetic experts across the country to study it.

Reply: Thank you very much for Mr. Ge's instructions丨However, there are some things that I dare not agree with. The reply is as follows: ㈠ The reasons why "all problems and difficulties are not individual" have been seen in the origin of this column published one day, and as Mr. Ge cited, the example of "difficulties in chemistry or physics" especially clearly shows that this kind of academic doubt cannot be unique to individuals. ㈡ It is of course possible to disclose the names of experts, but it is not necessary. ㈢ Mr. Liu Tingfang's statement in his letter, "Not to degenerate into the kind of three hundred solutions to opening skills and difficult problems," originally meant to hope that this column's vibrant garden would not degenerate into a rigid and barren land like an account book. "Three hundred solutions to arithmetic problems" is a metaphor. ㈣ Not every problem is proposed for discussion. Only some of the more important problems are proposed for discussion. Arithmetic problems are naturally handed over to experts to answer.

Weather Report 154

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday said that Shandong, Zhouwei, and the Yellow Sea are cloudy and cloudy with snow, colder and with fairly strong northwest winds. The coast here and above the East China Sea are mostly cloudy and clear, cold and with fairly strong northeast winds. There are cyclones around the Ryukyu Islands due to the hurricane southeast south of Naha moving northeast-north. The weather between Taiwan and Little Luzon is very bad due to another hurricane east of Luzon moving northwest or northwest-north. The Yangtze River basin is cloudy with northwest winds. The center point of the first hurricane at 6:00 AM was within sixty miles of the intersection of 15 degrees north latitude and 124 degrees east longitude, moving northwest, and the wind force is unknown. The second hurricane was at noon within sixty miles of the intersection of 21 degrees north latitude and 130 degrees east longitude, moving northeast-north, and the wind force is very strong. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 46.9 and the lowest was 34.3. On the same day last year, the highest was 67.1 and the lowest was 45.5.

Education News

Important News 156

Su Education Commissioner Zhou Fohai Inspects Northern Jiangsu Record (4)

Calls Together Elementary School Teachers and Staff for Instruction

Proceeds from Inspection of Schools to Rugao

(Nantong Dispatch) Su Education Commissioner Zhou Fohai's three-day inspection of Nantong has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that Zhou summoned elementary school teachers and educational administrators on the evening of the 3rd of this month, with more than 200 people attending. The general idea of the instruction was that there are generally three problems with local education in Jiangsu Province: one is exhaustion, two is disputes, and three is waste. However, Nantong is generally still good, but the self-closure and lack of research in the education sector urgently need to be continuously improved. There are three things I would like to encourage my colleagues with: first, do not save trouble. It is a mistake to say that it is better to do one less thing than one more thing. Second, do not be afraid of trouble. It is also wrong to say that you do not seek merit but seek no fault, because no merit is fault. If you are truly causing disputes for the sake of reforming education in Huai, you should take full responsibility, and I will do my best to protect you. Third, do not make mistakes. The ancients said that you should think before you act, and this sentence is extremely valuable. Educational administrators and teachers should cooperate and divide their work. Educational administrators should do their best to raise funds, and teachers should not neglect their own duties because of insufficient funding. I hope everyone will work together with the spirit of what I said before, "two people eat one person's meal and one person does two people's work," under the current situation where education funding is extremely difficult. Chen, the section chief, then stated that Nantong education has three advantages: ㈠ Solid foundation, ㈡ No factions or localism, ㈢ Teachers and staff are dedicated, and students can study hard. However, there are also two points to note: ㈠ Pay attention to physical education, ㈡ Have a sense of initiative. Regarding universal education, the education department has three methods: ㈠ Supplementing school enrollment, ㈡ Township and towns should establish junior primary schools, ㈢ Improving private schools. The above three items will be promulgated with detailed measures soon, and each county must hold a publicity week for improving private schools, hoping that colleagues in the education sector will cooperate. Section Chief Xiang then stated that there are two contributions to Nantong's school education: ㈠ Emphasize the cultivation of elementary school children, and should not simply impart knowledge. ㈡ Teachers and staff should continue to study academics and teaching methods. There is also one request, which is to cooperate with social education. As for social education: ㈠ The work should be practical, ㈡ It should be deeply rooted in the masses. Finally, the director of the Education Bureau replied on behalf of the administration and dispersed. On the morning of the 4th, Zhou and his party went to the Daquan Yarn Factory Deputy Factory to visit and inquired in detail about the improvement of cotton seeds, factory equipment, and labor treatment. They then inspected the rural primary schools at Baitang Temple and Cao Gong Temple, visited the historical sites of Nantong. Visited the farmers' homes at the Japanese Tomb and took a group photo. I heard the sound of looms in the fields, which was very admirable, saying that Nantong truly deserves the name of a model county. They then went to the School for the Blind and Deaf, where the blind and deaf students welcomed them in teams and performed martial arts, with lively spirits, which was very pitiful. Zhou immediately donated one hundred yuan to reward them. After leaving the school, they went to Zhang Jian's tomb and traveled around the five mountains. That night, they stayed at the Sanyuan Palace in Langshan. On the 5th, at 8 o'clock, they attended the Tongzhong Anniversary Week in heavy rain and gave instructions. They continued to inspect the Education Bureau, Commercial Middle School, and visited the Nantong College of Science, Hospital, and Museum. They left Nantong at 2 PM to go to Rugao.

Standards for Kindergarten and Elementary School Curricula Promulgated by the Ministry of Education (50) 157

Manual Arts

First, Goals

㈠ To cultivate children's laboring skills and the spirit of equality, mutual assistance, and cooperation.

㈡ To develop children's planning and creative abilities.

㈢ To increase children's interest and ability in production and to inspire their aspirations and knowledge to improve life, agriculture, or industry.

Second, Types of Work

㈠ School Affairs: The principle of using fewer school workers should be followed. All school affairs, large and small, should be discussed by the children and teachers together, and the work methods should be assigned separately. The teachers must examine the consequences.

㈡ Household Affairs: Schools with better household equipment should focus on working in the school. If the equipment is lacking, the work can be arranged in the school and the work methods can be discussed. The operation is limited to the household, and the teachers find ways to examine the results. The scope of work focuses on food, clothing, and shelter.

㈢ Agricultural Affairs: In addition to remote arts, which must be operated in the school, this type of work must be available in rural or urban areas. Planting and animal husbandry should be set up in rural elementary schools. If it cannot be set up, the scope of work can be specified in the school, and the working methods can be studied. The family is limited to being an assistant to the father and brother, and the teacher finds ways to examine the results. The scope is: 1. Gardening: Studying the planting of local major vegetables and common flowers and fruit trees must be combined with the work of the natural science department to form an entire unit. If it is absolutely unavoidable, the content of the course can be reduced and changed to "potted plants." 2. Farming: Studying the cultivation of local major crops and the improvement of agricultural tools and new cultivation methods, and studying the improvement of farmers' lives. 3. Animal Husbandry: Raising local common poultry, livestock, and silkworms, bees, fish, etc., and studying and experimenting with new animal husbandry methods.

㈣ Industry: Focus on making and studying local special crafts. Schools that focus on agricultural affairs can omit this work if they cannot have both. Each school can set up the following crafts as much as possible according to environmental needs and abilities. Senior grade students need to do one or two things: ㈠ Special products and crafts, such as straw hats in Shandong, straw hats and woven mats in Ningbo, Zhejiang... All those that children can do are set up in the school, or children are limited to helping their fathers and brothers operate at home. The teachers examine the results. ㈡ Paper crafts: making paper flowers, books, toys, models, stationery, furniture, etc., and understanding the lives of such workers. ㈢ Earthwork: Operation of toys, models, stationery, bricks, tiles, etc., and understanding, investigation, and research of the lives of such workers. ㈣ Carpentry: making toys, models, stationery, furniture, etc., and understanding, investigation, and research of the lives of such workers. ㈤ Metalwork: making toys, armor, etc., and understanding, investigation, and research of the lives of such workers.

Fourth, Teaching Points: Drawing and other methods of practice

㈠ This subject should fully combine with social and natural joint teaching, and should fully apply the design of single units, such as "Toy Life" in Grades 1 and 2, "Original Life" or "Foreign Life" in Grades 3 and 4, etc. as a teaching method

㈡ Investigating local specialties and choosing to use them as teaching materials is a major task of labor education

㈢ The real environment, such as family factories, shops, fields, villages, transportation agencies, etc., is a reference for labor methods and a large source of labor materials. Cheap or free real objects and pieces should be fully utilized, such as advertising products, advertising paintings, sample cloths, furniture factories' useless equipment, crops that can be obtained from farms... They should also be fully collected for application, and children should be encouraged to refer to and collect them themselves

㈣ On-site operations and investigations are most prone to fatigue due to labor. Fully utilize methods such as achievement competitions to encourage children to work hard

㈤ Before on-site operation and investigation, children must be fully planned to make children budget, so that the methods, time, and materials used are economical and effective

㈥ During on-site operation, it is necessary to pay attention to whether the child can operate according to the prior plan, correct his mistakes at any time, assist him with what he cannot do, and guide them with economical and ingenious methods, but the child's freedom of expression should not be encroached upon

㈦ After the on-site operation and investigation are completed, the shortcomings must be criticized, the merits and demerits of the achievements must be compared, and the children must be informed of their progress

㈧ Emphasize joint operations to cultivate a spirit of cooperation

㈨ Discussion and research must be integrated with operation and investigation, and must not be an independent operation and become empty talk

㈩ Appropriate materials for appreciation can be provided to increase children's artistic interest. Stories about the invention of things can also be lectured or introduced to children at appropriate times

㈩㈠ The power of children in Grades 1 and 2 is limited, so attention should be paid to the work process and good results should not be demanded

㈩㈡ In Grades 3 and 4, children should be fully empowered to use their own power to meet their own needs. Guidance on working methods, tool management, repair, and usage methods must be emphasized

㈩㈢ In Grades 5 and 6, although children should be urged to strictly apply working methods to achieve excellent results, the economical process, ingenious creativity is still more important than excellent results

Regulations on Social Education Institutions in Jiangsu Province 158

Eight Already Approved

Two Still to be Formulated

The Ministry of Education yesterday consulted the Jiangsu Provincial Government that the ten provisional regulations on the organization of social education institutions in Jiangsu Province previously approved and sent for consultation, except for the provisional regulations on the organization of county-level lecture halls in Jiangsu Province and the provisional regulations on the appointment, removal, and treatment of directors, should be transferred to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education for separate formulation (the scope is too large, such as the director having five directors below, which is difficult to implement. The director does not need to submit a request to the Department of Education for appointment. It can be visited by the public school principal's office and hired by the competent county educational administrative agency). The remaining eight have been filed by the department.

More than 800 students at Jinan University 159

Ministry of Education previously inspected report of more than 500 people

The Ministry of Education previously sent personnel to inspect Jinan University. The inspection report stated that there were more than 500 students at Jinan University. According to the school's statement, there are still students who are not divided into colleges, totaling more than 800 people. The Ministry of Education verified the situation and found that it was correct and approved the filing, and recognized that the school did have more than 800 people.

Schools Purchase National Crisis Photo Series 160

The Ministry of Education received a letter from the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan, stating that Xu Tonglai, a representative of the Shanghai Self-Strengthening Society, requested that schools be instructed to purchase the National Crisis Photo Series (photos of the Shanghai 19th Route Army resisting Japan and the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army). The case was handed over to the Ministry of Education for handling. The Ministry of Education yesterday sent letters to the Departments of Education of various provinces, the competent education authorities of various cities, public and approved private colleges and universities, and the Weihaiwei Commissioner's Office, requesting that they instruct their subordinates to purchase the National Crisis Photo Series as appropriate.

City Education Association's Telegram to the National Education Community to Aid the Righteous Army 163

The Righteous Army's Telegrams and Letters Requesting Aid are as Urgent as Flying Sparks; Our Nation's People Share the Same Hatred of the Enemy, How Can We Bear to Sit Idle?

The Shanghai City Education Association telegraphed the national education community, stating through the Shanghai newspaper offices to all provincial and municipal education associations: "Regrettably, since the fall of the Northeast, over a year has swiftly passed. The Japanese invaders have been employing treacherous schemes but have failed to govern the Northeast, and their puppet government's organization has failed to establish a foundation. This is all due to the righteous volunteers of the Northeast shedding blood and fighting! The spirit of our righteous volunteers sacrificing for the nation is truly enough to surpass the past and present, and move heaven and earth. However, after years of bloody battles, they have endured many hardships, and the supplies needed by the troops are often insufficient. To achieve complete success, they rely on rear support. Now, the north wind roars, the frontier is bitterly cold, and ice and snow rage. Funding is scarce, and letters and telegrams requesting aid are as urgent as flying sparks. Moreover, the enemy and rebels are pressing in with large forces, and fierce battles have already begun. Assistance is even more urgent. Our nation's people share the same hatred of the enemy. How can we bear to sit idle and remain indifferent? In the past, the fundraising movement to aid the righteous volunteers has risen like a storm in various places. We colleagues in the education community, being intellectuals, how can we be willing to fall behind? Based on this principle, our association convened a meeting of representatives from major primary and secondary schools across the city on November 23, and passed eight fundraising methods. Since actively promoting fundraising from November 25, the results have been remarkable, demonstrating that saving the country is the common desire of all people. We have long admired your association's leadership of education throughout the province and city. If you can raise your voice from a high place, it will surely be like... Therefore, we hope that everyone will work together to overcome difficulties, and the future of the country will truly depend on it. Respectfully submitting this telegram for your consideration. Seal of the Shanghai City Education Association."

County Education Bureau Bureau Affairs Meeting 164

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 268th bureau affairs meeting at the bureau at 2 PM yesterday. Attendees included Bureau Chief Shi, Lin Weiwen, Niu Zhiyi, Yang Huiming, Zheng Guo, Shen Jingzhi, Shao Yuan, Zhonghou, Xi Siwu, Wu Qing, etc. Chairman Shi, Recording Secretary Xi Siwu. The meeting was opened as scheduled, and the following matters were discussed: ㈠ The case regarding the date of the winter regular meeting of the current administrative committee was discussed and decided to be held at 2 PM on December 28. ㈡ The case in which Educational Committee Member Niu forwarded the request of Wu Zhaozhi Primary School to raise funds to add classrooms and planned to repay the association's loan in installments with tuition income for record-keeping was discussed and decided to be feasible in fact. However, using operating expenses to repay the association's loan can only be used to offset the surplus amount, and the original tuition fees must not be diverted, which would hinder the budget. ㈢ The case in which Educational Committee Member Niu forwarded the request of Wu Zhaozhi Primary School to add classes and hire a formal teacher in the elementary school period for verification was discussed and decided that it involved adjustments to the budget and was difficult to approve. It should be handled again when the annual budget is prepared. ㈣ The case in which Educational Committee Member Niu reviewed the report that Peicai Primary School in the second district used purchased civilian houses as school buildings was discussed and decided to send a letter to the Second District Office to judge that the civilian houses were not suitable and should be postponed. ㈤ The case in which Educational Committee Member Niu forwarded the request for the allocation of temporary funds for Xinmin Primary School was discussed and decided that there were no funds available and it was difficult to approve. ㈥ The case in which Tangwan Minjiao Yi presented the organizational charter of the member committee and requested verification was discussed and decided to revise and implement it. The meeting was adjourned.

Examination of "Combat," "Wrestling," "Fencing," and "Bayonet Fighting" (Part 2) 171

(Former Training Director and Editor of the Jiangsu Provincial Martial Arts Hall)

— Jin Yiming

㈢ Fencing

"Fencing" is the art of striking and stabbing with a sword. The Book of Han, Sima Xiangru, Xiangru, studied "fencing" while reading. Later generations used knives to... "chop and stab". The Spring and Autumn Annals of Wu and Yue records that Yue Nu saw the King of Yue "King of Yue" and said: "What about the way of the sword?" The woman said: "I was born in the deep forest and grew up in the uninhabited wilderness. I have no way to learn or... The princes secretly like the way of striking and reciting it endlessly. I did not receive it from others, but suddenly I have it myself." King Yue said: "How is the way?" The woman said: "The way is very subtle and easy, and its meaning is profound and deep. The way of hand-to-hand combat is "internal reality, spirit, and external appearance of peace and ceremony." "Seeing it is like sweeping well, and seizing it is like fearing a tiger." One person is equal to a hundred, and a hundred people are equal to ten thousand. This statement deeply captures the essence of "fencing." From this, we can know the origin of "fencing" in our country has been around for a long time.

Zhuangzi's Saying on Swords discusses the way of the sword, saying that one must "show it with emptiness and open it with profit," "follow it with development and arrive first." The words are simple but the meaning is comprehensive and deeply insightful. The Biography of Jing Ke says that Goujian heard that Jing Ke's assassination of the King of Qin failed and privately said: "Alas, what a pity that he did not study the art of stabbing with a sword." This shows that the art of fencing in the past had reached a profound level. Even Jing Ke was said to have not studied the art of stabbing with a sword, implying that later generations only knew how to carry a zither and sword box, and could play the zither but could not fence. Emperor Wen of Wei's Preface to the Dian Lun said that he learned "fencing" when he was young, and he had many teachers. The methods of the four directions were the best in the capital. At the same time, Mr. Liu was also good at "fencing". He Liangchen's Chen Ji of the Ming Dynasty said: "The disorderly patterns of Zhuangzi, the rise and fall of the Law King, the response law of Mr. Liu, the lightning law of Black Ming Wang, and the methods of dispatching troops by Ma Qi, the sword skills of these five families may or may not have been passed down." From this, we know that there were not many skilled "fencing" experts in the Ming Dynasty. Therefore, He Liangchen felt that the so-called swordsmanship of the five families must also have some basis. The Sword Classic attached to Qi Jiguang's Jixiao Xinshu is a transcription of what Yu Dayou wrote. Dayou learned "Jingchu long sword" from Li Liangqin, so the principles described in his sword classic are to transform the sword skills into stick skills, and he said that stick skills are like the Four Books, and knives and guns are like the Six Classics. If one can master the stick, then the methods of various stabbing weapons can be obtained from this. I compare boxing to character blocks, and sticks, knives, guns, and swords to reading books, especially swords with double blades are the most difficult of the four. As for the length and size of the sword, I have seen detailed records in the examinations. The Knife and Sword Record records the year numbers of the past dynasties and the names of the swords that were made, which can also be verified one by one. These two books can also be seen in old bookstores.

㈣ Bayonet Fighting

The General Examination of Literature records that the families who use spears have seventeen different methods, and the spear methods are also different. The Yang family's twenty-six roads of flowered spear, the Ma family's spear, the Zha family's spear, the Zhang Fei spear, the Five Manifestations Divine Spear, the Crutch Spear, the Crutch Blade Spear, the Javelin Spear, the Hammer Spear, the Renning Brush Spear, the Anti-Horse Spear, the Surprise Spear, the Emei Spear, the Sha family's eighteen strikes, the inverted pole, the Golden Dart, and the Ground Tongue Spear, totaling seventeen types. The Biography of Wang Yanzhang in the History of the Five Dynasties says that Yanzhang was brave and powerful, able to walk barefoot on thorns for a hundred steps, holding an iron spear and riding and speeding, rushing forward as fast as flying, and others could not hit him. The army called him Wang Iron Spear. The Biography of Li Quan in the History of the Song Dynasty says that Quan was agile in archery and horsemanship, and could wield a lance. At the time, he was known as Li Iron Spear. His wife, Zhao, said to Zheng Yande: "For twenty years, the pear blossom spear has been invincible under heaven." Later, Qi Jiguang trained soldiers, taking the essence and removing the dross from the Yang family's spear methods, and adopted the General Remarks on Long Spears. It says that the method of the long spear began with the Yang family, and it is called the pear flower. The world admires it. The key is to be familiar with it. "If you are familiar with it, your heart can forget your hand, and your hand can forget the spear, round and spiritual without stagnation. It is also most important to be quiet." If you are quiet, your heart will not move rashly, and you can deal with it calmly, with unpredictable changes and infinite divinity." The methods that are practiced in the world today are all the methods of the Sha family and the Ma family. The Sha family's pole and the Ma family's long spear each have their own wonderfulness and have differences in length. Their use is only the method of the Yang family, which has reality and falsehood, and has oddity and uprightness. Its advance is sharp and its retreat is fast, its momentum is dangerous and its section is short. It does not move like a mountain, and it moves like thunder. Therefore, it is said that the pear blossom spear has been invincible under heaven for twenty years. Chen Ji's Yang family's pear blossom spear is better than the Zha family's spear, the Sha family's pole, and the Li family's short spear. However, Qi Dongmou said that it is different when applied to the marching array. Its meaning is that when facing a large array, strength must not be given priority, and weakness must not be given priority. When using the spear, the method should be simple and the establishment should be sparse. If it is not simple, it will not be able to distinguish disputes, and if it is not sparse, it will not be able to observe and move forward and retreat. This is the main force of the spear method used in the battlefields of the past.

Now, the Central Martial Arts Hall adopts "bayonet fighting" as the great spear, but "splitting and stabbing" is still unknown. Only the spear is the main weapon, and the spear method says, "Your spear stabs me, I strike your spear. If your spear doesn't move, my spear will fire. The spear is... the waist lock is the first to stab the hands and feet. The high doesn't stab, the side doesn't save the middle. Don't be afraid of the empty spear. It's difficult to lift the stand with one spear. If you circle, I will also circle, but I'm afraid that the hand is too late to go like an arrow and come like a line, pointing at people's throats and wrinkled faces, and stabbing people without seeing it.

Master Fu Chuanru once told me the song and decision, saying, "When using the spear at Chen Shi, the sun is in the east, occupying the east to commit adultery and use attack. When using the spear at noon, the sun is in the south, don't teach the sun to meet you with both spears. When using the spear at You Shi, the sun is in the west, occupying the west to see the height. When using the spear in June, you must avoid the sun, and when using the spear in December, you must avoid the wind." I have carefully described what I know. I hope that martial arts comrades will advance and teach it.

Important Notice from the Chinese Football Association 172

丨Regarding Uniform Reports and Player Matters丨

㈠ Each team's players must wear the same jersey with numbers on the back to be allowed to play. Each team manager is fully responsible for this matter and must ensure that there are no mismatched jerseys in the team to maintain a good appearance and the spirit of the association. If a team's jerseys are not uniform, the referee on the field has the right to refuse to start the game. Please take note.

㈡ The game report form should be submitted to the referee by each team manager immediately after the end of the game. It should not be delayed. The form should be filled in carefully and accurately for reference.

㈢ Matters such as using unregistered members or impostor players to join the game, or each member registering for two teams or joining two teams to play are related to sportsmanship and the reputation of the team. The person in charge of the team should pay close attention. If they knowingly violate the rules, they will be found to be despicable and immediately have their membership in the association revoked. If the supervisors in the association have conclusive evidence that such matters have been found in any team, they should file a protest and report to the association to maintain the spirit of the association.
