Donglu Wins Junior Football Championship 178

(Jinan Communication) The Shandong Provincial Public Sports Field launched the winter football and basketball competition in 1932, divided into men's senior football and basketball, men's junior football and basketball, and women's basketball, which began on October 19th. This winter's weather is mild, which is a good football and basketball season. However, due to the student unrest, many men's senior football and basketball teams have withdrawn from the competition in the past two weeks, which is a pity. This week is the third week. Men's senior football and basketball, men's junior basketball, and women's basketball are divided into groups for round-robin matches due to the large number of participating teams. It will take two weeks to finish. However, only three schools participated in the men's junior football, and the first round-robin match was used. Donglu Junior High School defeated Provincial No. 1 Vocational School 12-0 in the first week, and then defeated Qilu Junior High School 7-0 this week, winning this year's championship and maintaining the honor of the 1931 winter football tournament. The other championships will be determined in two weeks. Judging from the results of the three weeks, those who compete for the men's senior football championship should belong to Jingcheng and the senior department of Qizhong. Boai defeated Qida this week and has hope of winning the basketball championship. The men's junior basketball championship is expected to be won by No. 1 Middle School Zhiyi, and the women's basketball championship may belong to the Women's Normal School. Now I will describe the battle between Donglu and Qizhong this week.

Donglu Wins Qizhong At 3:00 PM in the afternoon, the two sides entered the field to practice shooting and passing. The referee, Wan Ruzhang Ziyao, blew the silver whistle. Qizhong was in the south and Donglu was in the north. Donglu attacked first. After the kick-off, Qizhong took the lead. Donglu reorganized its troops and launched a counterattack, repeatedly attacking the city. Then, Donglu drove straight in and brought the ball into the goal. At the end of the first half, Donglu won four goals, all brought into the goal. At the beginning of the second half, Qizhong tried to counterattack and was full of energy. It attacked Donglu's goal several times, but the shots were weak and were easily thrown out by Donglu's goalkeeper. Donglu reorganized its troops and advanced again. Qizhong's forwards retreated and defended desperately. Donglu's center repeatedly dribbled the ball to the goal, but failed to succeed. Finally, Qizhong's two goals were too weak and the gate was unable to prevent Donglu from scoring two consecutive goals. Before 30 minutes, they scored another goal. Then, the silver whistle blew and the war ended. The final result was 7-0, Donglu won. Donglu won the first vocational school. Qizhong won the championship. The first vocational school defeated Qizhong 2-1 and won the runner-up. The junior football ended here.

Ocean Silver Tael Fell in the Morning, Rebounded in the Afternoon 185

Ocean Silver Tael Money Market Slightly Better by 1 Fen

Yesterday, the ocean silver market was sluggish in the morning due to a lack of buying interest, resulting in a fall of 7 hao and a half. In the afternoon, banks bought in, boosting market sentiment, and eventually it was better than the previous day. The market conditions are listed below:

Interest Rate 186

Ways to Order Foreign Wheat · Zhi · De 198

The huge amount of foreign wheat shipped in recent years has occupied a very important position in imported goods, second only to rice, with a value of hundreds of millions. The decline in domestic wheat production is undeniable, and the encouragement of production by overseas wheat-producing countries has led to a surge in production, and the method of dumping has to be used. My country's tariff barriers are weak and have been subjected to foreign economic aggression for a long time. Free competition has been unrestrictedly. Looking back, wheat production has declined to an incalculable level. Recently, if the factories do not import foreign wheat, they will all shut down. The serious state has already been seen. It is better to have major agricultural provinces, either suffering from the disaster of soldiers and bandits, or suffering from water and drought disasters, or even suffering from bad politics

The oppression of fertile farmland is changed to planting panic, the agricultural time is lost, and the production is less. Recalling the time of the Republic of China, Sichuan Province

The amount of wheat arriving in Shanghai was about 300,000 to 400,000. At that time, the Shanghai flour factory was just starting, and the cheap wheat and expensive flour created a boom. Subsequently, the wheat production in Henan (the most) and Hubei provinces was concentrated in Hankou and came to Shanghai one after another. The Anhui North area is also a rich wheat-producing area, and most of Shanghai is the end. Knowing that after 20 years, Sichuan is nothing

Even Hankou wheat is almost extinct. The wheat from Anhui coming from the Grand Canal and the Yangtze River is not as smooth as before the Republic of China. Accumulating this kind of flour mills in the port, except for the new wheat season, can still cope, otherwise, they must rely on foreign wheat. Today, they have formed a panic that cannot be maintained without the import of foreign wheat. This kind of food crisis for the people cannot be solved without extremely good politics.

Calculation of Pricing The procedure for ordering foreign wheat is quite simple and the calculation is absolutely convenient. That is, the foreign quotation obtained by the foreign merchants and the exchange rate on the same day are converted into the number of guiyuan. If the two parties are close, the transaction can be concluded. It is determined to order American wheat and Canadian wheat. The wheat is numbered from 1 to 5, and 2 to 3 are the most. The foreign market price is based on each ton (ie 2,000 pounds) (equivalent to 15 dan) as a unit. Assuming that the quotation for American wheat is US$17 per ton (including water feet and commission, Shanghai delivery, starting at US$30 for exchange, converted into Shanghai guiyuan is 56 taels, 6 qian and 6 fen, divided by 15 dan to get 3 taels, 7 qian and 8 fen per dan in Shanghai guiyuan). If you want to order Canadian wheat, you can also use this method. The only difference between Canadian wheat and American wheat is that American wheat is 2,000 pounds per ton, while Canadian wheat is 2,240 pounds (ie 16 dan and 80 jin). When ordering wheat from various ports in Australia, it is not divided into grades, but the weight of each bushel (British container) is used as the standard. Ordinary goods weigh 60 pounds, followed by 58 pounds, and as high as 62 pounds. When ordering, both parties specify a pound amount, and the order indicates that if there is insufficient weight upon arrival, there are official regulations that lower the price. The calculation method assumes that each British pound (2,240 pounds) is 5 pounds, 4 shillings and 6 pence, which is 1,254 pence. Assuming an exchange rate of 1 shilling and 9 pence, it is equal to 59 taels, 7 qian and 1 fen in Shanghai guiyuan. Divide by 16 dan and 80 jin to get 3 taels, 5 qian and 5 fen and zero (price per dan). If the futures quotations for Chicago Canadian foreign wheat are mentioned, the industry generally calculates 333, and most people in the 333 principle are unclear. It must be known that 333 is 33.3 bushels (the first bushel of 60 pounds is suitable for 2,000 pounds). This is different from the nature of spot goods for the futures standard price. Because the spot price and the standard are often inconsistent, it is just a trend for the industry to understand. (To be continued)

Free Talk

Rouge 216

— Shi Heng

One afternoon, I went to visit a contemporary famous painter, Mr. S.

The painter was working at his desk. Seeing me, he didn't put down his brush, but his mouth was entertaining me. He told many stories about painting. I don't understand art, so I just listened to him silently. He occasionally mentioned the so-called genius of art. I have never believed in any kind of genius, so I slightly refuted him. The painter put down his brush and began to seriously discuss the issue of genius with me.

His argument failed to convince me because I am someone who absolutely does not easily abandon my own views.

Finally, Mr. S, with a contemptuous look, began to tell a story.

"Once upon a time, there was a painter (the person telling the story mentioned a very familiar name, but I forgot it)," he began, "who was the best at painting beauties. But his works were rarely appreciated."

"One day, a powerful person held a grand banquet, inviting countless contemporary literati and artists. This painter was of course invited as well."

"At the appointed time, he arrived. During the banquet, they talked about many anecdotes about literati or painting. When they talked about the present, everyone praised his skill in painting beauties. So the painter, in a triumphant mood, drank a few more glasses of wine and was already somewhat drunk."

"After the banquet, the host suggested leaving a souvenir, asking each of the literati and painters present to show off their skills. Some wrote poems, some painted, and finally it was his turn to paint a beauty. But he was drunk, dazedly and vaguely listening to the praises of the people around him. He was a little afraid. He was afraid that under the influence of alcohol, he would not be able to paint a meticulous masterpiece."

"People urged him, and he was still hesitating. Finally, with trembling hands, he picked up the brush. He began to draw the outline of a young woman's face on the prepared white paper. Hazy eyes and trembling hands could not do as he wished. He felt a little annoyed. He hated the people around him who were forcing him to write."

"After finishing the face, he didn't want to continue painting. Now, the young woman's face on the white paper, seen through his drunken eyes, had no vitality at all. His annoyance shifted to the person in the painting."

He thought to himself that the existence of this young woman's face would ruin his reputation, and he became even more angry.

"Picking up the brush again, he applied thick ink and brushed it twice on the face. As if mad, under the dumbfounded gaze of the crowd, he strode away."

"All night, the painter couldn't sleep, remorse tormenting his heart. He even thought that he would never pick up a brush again."

"The next morning, as he was painfully tossing and turning in bed, he heard a chaotic sound of people outside the house. His friends pulled him out of bed."

"It turned out that his friends had come specifically to congratulate him on his success last night. Last night, after he ran away in a frenzy, people didn't understand his mood. After being stunned for a while, they all turned their eyes to the young woman's face. At this time, they discovered a miracle. The two strokes of thick ink that he wanted to use to destroy the face in anger appeared on the young woman's cheeks, just like two thick dabs of rouge, and these two dabs of rouge made the face even more vivid, surpassing the achievements of all his previous beauty paintings."

"From then on, in addition to his reputation for being good at painting beauties, the painter also gained a reputation for being good at painting rouge."

Mr. S finished his story here. He further argued:

"Do you still not believe in the so-called genius of art? You must explain this story as accidental. Yes, it is indeed accidental, but why can this kind of accident only happen in the hands of that painter?"

I stared blankly, smoking a cigarette. I had no words to answer him.

November 30, 1935

Freedom 217

— Hành

"Freedom," in this world, it is said to truly exist. However, after all, its nature is too mysterious and wonderful, vague and indistinct, like a wisp of green smoke, or like a sweet dream. As soon as you reach out, the smoke dissipates from your hand, and the dream vanishes from your memory. Your hand is empty, grasping nothing. Therefore, until now, "freedom" has remained just a faint shadow, seeming to exist yet not quite.

Nevertheless, the world is full of clever people. Occasionally, a kite soars into the sky, or a fish leaps out of the water. The clever people then exclaim with a sense of discovery: "Look, freedom is right here, actively present in this lively natural mechanism!" And even cleverer people declare with even greater certainty: "Give me not liberty, but give me death!"

But when it comes to death, it is ultimately not as easy as "a kite flying" or "a fish leaping." Sometimes, when you want to die, you are not allowed to. Just as when you want to live, you are not allowed to. "Not allowing you to live" is very easy to prove with an example right before our eyes, so there's no need to elaborate. And by the banks of the Huangpu River in Shanghai and on the Yanziji cliffs in Nanjing, it is said that stone tablets have been erected that read "Thou Shalt Not Die!" And suicide, it is said, violates some law, article so-and-so, number so-and-so. Hmph! Do you think you are free to die?

Even though the sea is so vast and the sky is so empty, kites and fish must still be constantly vigilant. Because among the myriad things, there is ultimately a distinction between "strong" and "weak." The strong can arbitrarily set up a fence on the sea surface and in the sky, forbidding you to fly, forbidding you to leap. If you want to act at all freely, you will very easily find yourself caught in a well-laid net!

Therefore, during the Qin Shi Huang era, no one dared to "whisper," nor did anyone dare to "collect books." Everyone suppressed themselves with all their might, pressing themselves flat and stuffing themselves into a wall crack that allows entry but no exit. This is because there was no one willing to reach out and grasp the ungraspable smoke, and death, after all, is somewhat frightening.

But the First Emperor's net was finally broken by the people in the wall cracks. Here, it cannot be said that "freedom" has truly been grasped, but if the people in the wall cracks break through a few more nets, perhaps one day when they reach out, their hand will not be forever empty!

Soviet Russian Kindergartens 218

— Ke Duo

Soviet Russian kindergartens are divided into many ethnic groups, such as Tatars, Cossacks, Ukrainians, and Glozhen. Each ethnic group has its own unique customs and habits, so children's education must be specially tailored to enable cultural education to be successful after they become adults. Children with illnesses, such as disabilities or deformities, are grouped separately and given appropriate education to facilitate correction. There are also ordinary children's groups. Each group is divided into day and night classes. Children whose parents work during the day are sent to the kindergarten in the morning and picked up in the evening; those whose parents work at night are sent to the kindergarten in the evening and picked up at midnight. Each group has two caregivers with quasi-teacher status who are dedicated to looking after them.

When children enter the kindergarten, they are first inspected by the caregivers to ensure they are clean. Children who are not clean are told to go to the washroom and wash themselves. Younger children are helped by the caregivers. Each child has their own washing utensils, such as soap, toothbrushes, and toothpaste. After everyone has finished washing, they put their utensils in a one-foot-high cupboard. Everything has its designated place, in an orderly manner, without any confusion. In the dining hall, there are chairs and tables specially designed for children, which they can easily move themselves. The plates, dishes, spoons, and cups are all very small. Each table has a class leader, elected by the children themselves. Mealtimes and tea times are supervised by the class leader and cared for by the caregivers, with very little squabbling over food. The furnishings in the club are similar to those in the playroom, but on a larger scale. The pictures on the walls are arranged in a very orderly manner, with portraits of Lenin in the center, and photographs of Soviet Russian celebrities such as Stalin and Molotov, as well as other slogans suitable for children, such as "Down with the family kitchen," "Make toys when young, build cars when old," "Help parents build socialism," "Complete the five-year plan in four years," and so on.

There is a special pharmacy for children's own use, containing iodine, boric acid ointment, bandages, cotton wool, rubber plaster, and so on. If a child has a minor injury, another child will apply the medicine and bandage it for them.

In addition, there are many small workshops, such as woodworking, carpentry,

, painting, and sand casting. The tools are also specially made and children can work on whatever they want. There are also models of airplanes and cars in the display room, which they can play with as they wish. The sports field is located outdoors and has various kinds of sports equipment for children. The equipment in the bedroom is similar to that in an infant ward, except that the beds are made of wood and have railings. The number of people sleeping in each bedroom is determined by the doctor based on the size of the room. Older children must make their own beds when they get up. The music room has various kinds of musical instruments for children to use, and they are allowed to play whatever instrument they like, without being stopped by the caregivers.

The daily routine of the children is as follows: 7:30 am wake up (children who do not live in the kindergarten enter between 7:30 am and 8:00 am), 8:00 am wash, 8:30 am breakfast, 9:00 am work. The type of work is determined by age. Work time is 40 minutes. At 10:00 am, they go for a walk in the garden or play various games in the sports field. At 11:00 am, they return to the kindergarten. At 12:00 pm, they have lunch and wash. 12:30 pm is nap time. 2:30 pm wake up, 3:00 pm work, 4:00 pm have snacks, and after 4:00 pm is playtime. 7:30 pm go home, earlier in winter and spring. 8:00 pm dinner. The equipment and layout in the kindergarten are very perfect. There are children's education experts in charge of the kindergarten affairs, and they often hold meetings and talks with the children's parents to discuss how to improve children's education. The local education committee supervises the kindergarten. Sometimes, staff from the kindergarten lead children to visit nearby factories, workshops, farms, or museums.

Most of the kindergarten's expenses are borne by the state. The children's parents only pay a small amount of money, or it is completely free for families in difficult circumstances.

Kindergartens also sign contracts with each other to compete with each other, and the good things are published in newspapers to attract children who have not yet entered the kindergarten.

Kindergarten children are from three to eight years old. Children over the age of eight are sent to elementary school.

× × × ×

The Heredity of Talent 219

— Sheng

Much of a person's talent is inherited. For example, musical talent is often evident from a young age. This is undoubtedly due to genetic inheritance. German composer Johann Sebastian Bach (1685-1750) had reached a level of maturity in his musical talent by the age of twenty-two. Beethoven at thirteen, and Mendelssohn Felix (1809-1847) at fifteen, both published their compositions. Furthermore, Austrian composer Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart (1756-1791) was able to compose at the age of five.

The Bach family produced more than twenty famous musicians, as well as more than forty ordinary musicians. This cannot but be attributed to heredity.

The precise heredity of musical talent has not yet been fully understood. According to Harst, the hereditary factor for music is recessive rather than dominant. Based on a comprehensive study of a large number of families, the hereditary situation is as follows:

(1) If both parents have special musical talent (whether vocal or instrumental), then their children may have special musical talent, or they may have ordinary musical talent.

(2) If neither parent has musical talent, and the grandparents (one or both) also lack musical talent, then none of the children will have musical talent.

(3) If one parent has special musical talent, and the other parent has ordinary musical talent, then their children's musical talent may be excellent, ordinary, or non-existent, in various combinations.

The World's Largest Ships Today 220

— Qiong

There are currently eight large ships in the world with a tonnage of over 40,000 tons. The longest of these is the British Majestic, which is 915 feet 5 inches long, with a total length from bow to stern of 954 feet 6 inches. This ship was originally the German Bismarck, but as a result of the war, it became British property.

In terms of tonnage, the American Leviathan is the largest, with 59,957 tons. This was originally the German Vaterland, which became American property after the war. It is 950 feet long, 104 feet high from keel to deck, has a draft of 39.5 feet, a displacement of 64,700 tons, can carry 3,400 passengers, and has a crew of 1,183 people. Its speed is 24 knots and its horsepower is 100,000. It carries approximately 9,300 tons of cargo. The walkways inside the ship are approximately two and a half miles long. There are 15,000 electric lights, with a total wire length of 5 miles. The chimney diameter is 32 feet. The fastest ships are the German Bremen and Europa. The planned speed of these two ships was originally 27 knots, but during testing, the average speed of both ships was over 28 knots. Their overall length is 938 feet 5 inches, their width is 101 feet 8 inches, their height is 97 feet 5 inches, their draft is 33 feet 7.5 inches, their horsepower is 92,500, they can carry 2,200 passengers, and the crew consists of 960 officers and sailors.

The purpose of building these two ships was to compete with Britain in crossing the Atlantic. The former took four days, seventeen hours, and forty-two minutes to cross the Atlantic, while the latter took four days, seventeen hours, and six minutes.

Long Novel

The Crossroads of Era and Love 7 221

— Zhang Ziping

Haiquan had to turn back and sit in a corner of the living room. He saw a servant carrying a basket of dry firewood and a small lead bucket of white coal, walking towards the stove.

"The young mistress instructed that because the weather is cold today, and you're from the South and might not be able to bear it, we should light the stove..." Haiquan didn't feel particularly cold, but he didn't stop him either.

(Four)

The curtains in the bedroom of Master Ren and his wife were still tightly drawn, not a single ray of sunlight could penetrate. A light blue gauze cover was added to the large electric lamp hanging from the center of the ceiling, emitting a kind of faint light like the autumn moon. The snow-white silk mosquito net still covered their bed. When the maid sent the visiting card in, she heard the sound of flirting laughter and whispers from the couple inside the net.

"Mr. Lin you mentioned the other day is here."

"Okay, please ask him to sit for a moment longer downstairs. We'll get up soon."

After the maid left, Peizhen struggled to get up, but Master Ren deliberately stopped her.

"Forget it. It's almost twelve o'clock."

She crawled out of the net, wearing a light peach-colored velvet pajama and a blue silk pants that reached just below the knees. She walked to the oval mirror stand, looked at her sleepy face, which had just woken up from a dream, to see if there were any flaws that shouldn't be seen by a man other than her husband. She looked at her face as she combed the tangled hair on her head. She smelled the fragrance of her hair. She thought, this is exactly one of the characteristics that her husband loves about her.

She began to wash, spending a full thirty minutes before finishing. At this time, her husband, Ren Jinhua, also got up and walked into the dressing room. He saw Peizhen concentrating on applying makeup in front of the vanity mirror, and couldn't help but stand behind her in a daze, stealing glances at her in the mirror.

"What are you looking at? Don't you recognize me?"

She stamped her foot and said coquettishly.

"You look even more beautiful today. Could it be..."

Jinhua smiled and picked up a toothbrush from the vanity, checking the Colgate toothpaste.

"You're talking nonsense again..."

She stretched her head back, and her whole body leaned against his chest.

"Go away, you're not allowed to be here!"

She said again in a spoiled tone. He ignored her and just kept smiling as he looked in the mirror.

"Stop fooling around, there's a guest downstairs. How can we keep him waiting?"

She finally stopped smiling and said to him seriously.

"I heard that your sister likes him a lot, he must be a handsome man, right? Is that why you're in such a hurry to see him?"

He said, finally letting go of her, allowing her to continue applying makeup.

After a while, she finished applying makeup and walked back to the room to change clothes. She chose a brightly colored plaid flannel qipao and her favorite pair of black patent leather high-heeled dancing shoes.

"I'll go downstairs and see what kind of handsome man he is..."

Discussions

Women 222

— Bai

People often talk about women. I think women are indeed worth talking about. A few days ago, it was said in the newspapers how French women are hardworking and thrifty, how Japanese women are patriotic and organize women's national defense corps, and how German women have gained status in society. These words are all true. Although French women love to apply rouge and powder, according to people who have lived there for a long time, at least 60 to 70 percent of French women are able to support themselves. After the war, there was an excess of women (here, let's use these two words tentatively). Especially when men choose spouses, their first condition is whether this woman can support herself.

Therefore, most women learn a profession during their single years, otherwise it is not easy to find a husband. It can be said that more than 90 percent of German women are able to support themselves. Looking back at Chinese women, we are truly beyond reach. Generally speaking, so-called educated modern women take reading as decoration in their girlhood, and luxury as glory. They go in and out of cinemas, dance halls, and social venues, considering themselves to be socialites. When they reach their twenties, they fall in love with a rich man, or a powerful noble, and become the wife of a celebrity, living a life more extravagant than that of queens and concubines.

On the man's side, regardless of wealth or poverty, the first condition for choosing a spouse is always the beauty of the face. As long as she is a flower-like maiden, he will marry her, even if he himself becomes a beast of burden, he will gladly endure it. This phenomenon has fostered the inferior nature of women relying on their husbands. Relying on their beautiful faces, they are not afraid of not finding a wealthy suitor.

Men, you all want to have a woman, right? And you want to have a so-called modern miss to be your woman, right? Before you have tasted her flavor, you are so passionately yearning for her, but I have to tell you, once you have her, you will add a lot of trouble. If you are a person with a bit of ambition, wanting to do something in this world, then it's terrible. Just her living expenses will be enough to make you dizzy and complain all day long.

If you raise a spoiled wife and don't want to become an official to make a fortune and squeeze the people's fat, you are truly the number one "wronged to death." Below that are those who, for the sake of their beautiful wives and concubines, become greedy and corrupt officials. In today's world, such people are everywhere, even schoolteachers, book writers, shop clerks, porters, and peddlers, few of whom are not slaves to women. Alas, women! However, the badness of women lies in men. Today, all the men in the country should issue an emergency general mobilization order. From this day and time onwards, regardless of beauty or ugliness, any woman who cannot support herself should not be taken as a wife. In this way, perhaps men will have some way out, and the so-called modern women will not dare to be coquettish and live their romantic lives any longer.

Science

Tram 223

— Tao Xiaotao

Trams are fast, convenient, and save money, so ordinary people like to ride them. Since we often ride them, how can we not know their principles? I will now introduce several tram principles below: (1) Rail tram

In the power plant, a generator is set up. When the generator rotates, it cuts across magnetic lines of force, generating current, which exits from the positive pole ↓

Overhead wires on the street ↓ Pole on the tram ↓ Starter box (the iron box in front of the driver) ↓ From the starter box ↓ DC motor at the bottom of the car ↓ Wheel and to the rail and back to the negative pole of the generator in the power plant. When the current reaches the motor, the motor rotates the wheels, and the car can move forward.

So how can the car be made to go faster or slower? This all depends on the function of the starter box. It can control the current from the generator, making it appropriate to determine the speed. In the starter box, there are metal strips, some with high resistance and some with low resistance. When you want the current to be weaker, you only need to connect the metal strip with high resistance to the circuit, and the current will be weaker. When you want the current to be stronger, you only need to connect the metal strip with low resistance to the circuit, and the current will be stronger. If you want to stop, you only need to disconnect the metal strip from the circuit, and the motor will stop when it does not receive current. The driver turns the wooden handle on the box with his hand, which means controlling the current. If you want the car to go backwards, you can only turn the small handle next to the large handle. This turn can cause current in the opposite direction to flow into the motor, causing the car to go backwards.

(2) Trolleybus

At first glance, trolleybuses are very strange. We may wonder, how can it run without a current circuit? But if you take a closer look at the differences between rail trams and trolleybuses, you will find their principle. Rail trams have a pole and an overhead wire; trolleybuses have two poles, and there are two overhead wires on top of it. One of its poles is equivalent to the function of the steel rail. When the current enters one pole from one overhead wire, to the motor, and from the other pole, the other overhead wire returns to the generator.

Sometimes the tram does not need overhead wires, and the electricity is hidden in the grooves of the track. This type of tram device does not yet exist in our country. Although it is more aesthetically pleasing on the surface, it is much more expensive.

Literature and Art

Titled to Zhang for Envoy to Nepal Conferment of Honors 224

— Sun Jingcheng

Nepal is located between Tibet and India, with pivotal importance. The National Government, due to the discord in Kangzang, feared that someone would induce Nepal to aid Tibet, so it specially sent Zhang Dingcheng as envoy to Nepal, carrying the Republic of China's gift of the Chinese Army General and First Class Baoding Medal to the Prime Minister and Grand Marshal of that country, as well as other gifts, to win them over. Therefore, I compose two seven-character regulated verses as follows:

Entrusted with credentials, an envoy sets out from China,

To confer medals and promote the general's grace.

In spring, the peaks rise high, viewing the Himalayas,

The distant star of the envoy illuminates the flowing sands.

Trust that Nepal will speak of reconciliation,

Zhang Qian is accustomed to sailing the raft.

Moreover, in years past, he served as a prominent official,

His praise extends to Java and India even now.

××××

Relying entirely on prestige to intimidate the heavens,

The jade bowl and pearl plate offer superior tactics.

Cease speaking of the Five Rams opening up the barbarous lands,

Do not covet the Eight Steeds and the grapes.

Wherever the imperial envoy arrives, soldiers and people rejoice,

Courtesy befitting the praise of the monarch and minister.

From now on, there is no need for western anxieties,

Across the vast ocean, ten thousand miles of tranquil winds and waves.

What is Love? 225

— Lan Ying

The Sacrifices of Zongcheng, Each with Their Own Merits

Thinking back to six years ago, when I was studying at M school, the students' conversations always revolved around the word "love." They researched and explored it as if it held endless fascination. In particular, Miss S from my class was the most eloquent, and could be considered the guide to love in our M school. At that time, I was only fifteen years old, and what did I know about love? Naturally, I had to ask the guide, Miss S! I asked her to tell me the meaning of love, but she seemed unwilling to answer me in detail. At this moment, her face flushed red, and she lowered her head. After a long time, she said, "You will naturally understand one day when you reach a suitable age." How strange, how could she see the word "love" as so mysterious, and didn't I have the qualifications to talk about love?

I remember one evening, my younger brother and I were strolling in V Park, and just as we were about to pass a large tree, the sound of a man and woman talking and laughing suddenly entered my ears. This wasn't anything particularly strange, but I felt that the woman's voice was very familiar. Listening more carefully, it turned out to be Miss S! This aroused my curiosity. Haha, how could they be talking and laughing in this dark place where the moon was obscured by the shadows of the trees? Ah, she's probably talking about love again. I quietly walked behind the tree and stood there, listening to everything they said. "Miss S, rest assured, I will never abandon you. I have ways to smooth things over with my family. If you don't believe me, we can exchange rings right away as a token of engagement." "Yes, I believe you very much. As long as you are determined to love me forever, I can certainly make my stubborn family agree to your request." In the quiet air, the two dark figures seemed to be exchanging tokens. I didn't understand what they were talking about, and I wanted to hear them talk more, but my little brother was already tugging at my clothes, indicating that he wanted to go home. I was afraid of being discovered, so I had to tiptoe away.

The next morning at school, I told my friend Miss W everything I had seen the night before, and asked her to tell me what it meant that Miss S was meeting with a man. She smiled slightly, and her electric gaze glanced at me from the corner of her eye. Then she tapped her finger on my forehead and said mockingly, "Little girl, what are you pretending to be all innocent and naive for? Go ask Miss S about her affairs, I don't know! But since she has this secret love, I must ask her to reveal it." With that, she took my hand and ran to Miss S's dormitory. Miss S, who was working at her desk, looked a little flustered when she saw us running in with smiles on our faces. She hurriedly stuffed a page of scarlet Western-style stationery that she had been writing on her desk into a drawer, but soon returned to her original state, although still with a forced, calm demeanor. Miss W saw her like this and understood her intentions, asking her, "Miss S, why are you writing love letters so secretly?" How could Miss S not defend herself? She then said, "Don't accuse me falsely! I can't find any lovers, maybe you're imagining things yourselves!" Miss W pointed at me and said, "Ask her! Who has a lover? Have you forgotten what happened in V Park last night? Haha, there's a witness here, what are you still denying? Tell the truth!" At this moment, Miss S's face flushed and paled, and her previous strong and unyielding demeanor had vanished without a trace, replaced by a shy and coy attitude, and she stared at us without saying a word. In this silent and tense atmosphere, I couldn't help but be reminded of my old question, and I mustered the courage to ask her, "Miss S, please reveal the process of your love, so that I can also learn the true meaning of love." Faced with such urging and coercion, she seemed to have no strength to resist at all, and could only agree to our request, saying, "Mr. C is a friend I made this spring. He works at L Company. I admire his mastery of writing, and he is also a talented musician. He loves me very much too, so we gradually moved from friendship to considering engagement and..." Her face flushed, and she could no longer continue speaking. But Miss W seemed to forgive her, saying, "Very good! When can we have the pleasure of attending your wedding feast?" She smiled slightly, and her facial expression was extremely smug. She didn't answer our question about when she and Mr. C would be living together, but from her smiling smugness, we could guess that the day of their union wasn't far off.

Miss S and Mr. C are now sweet lovers and will be a happy couple in the future. In the parks with trees and flowers, and in the cinemas showing movies, their footprints are often seen. Therefore, everyone in school knows about and envies this loving couple.

Time passed like flowing water, and four years have gone by in a flash. The romantic story of Mr. C and Miss S no longer exists in our minds, and who still pays attention to their actions? But unintentionally, we feel that Miss S this year is not as lively and happy as in previous years, but has become dull, sad, and depressed. If you look closely at her face, you can probably often find two deep tear streaks. How strange, what sad and unspeakable things has she experienced? I couldn't help but be reminded of my old trick of getting to the root of things, and I wanted to ask her, perhaps I could also relieve some of her pain. On this day, it happened to be Sunday, so I ran to Miss S's house to inquire about her sad affair. She endured the pain and said to me, "Men have no conscience. He used to say to me, 'If this marriage doesn't work out, I would rather not marry. Dear sister, I love you, I will never abandon you.' He used such sweet words to deceive me, a weak woman. Now, he hasn't even sent me a single letter. After inquiring through his friends, I learned that he had already gotten married a few months ago." Before she finished speaking, she was already crying like a river of tears. Seeing her so sad, I couldn't help but shed tears of sympathy. I comforted her for a while and then said goodbye and went home. I thought, what is love? It turns out to be the result of being deceived, resulting in such heartbreak. In the future, I'm afraid I won't dare to approach the word "love" because my best friend has suffered such pain. I heard this and was very sorry, so I recorded it here for everyone to taste what love is like.

Random Notes from Chonglou (2) 226

— Peng Nian

(1) A Judge with a Concubine Hearing a Case of Bigamy

What is the difference between a person with a concubine and a person committing bigamy? In theory and in law, there is a judgment, and I don't need to elaborate. However, I think a judge with a concubine will feel uneasy when hearing a bigamy case unless he is protected by the law. Why? Because he is also committing the same offense, which makes it more difficult to handle.

(2) Is it worth it to talk about morality in Shanghai?

Last night, Mr. Fei Fei and I went to Avenue Edward VII. When we passed Dongxin Bridge, we saw a group of bewitching "wild chickens" swarming around a villager. Coincidentally, there was a person dressed in 19th-century clothes in front of us, who said to his companion, "How can such a civilized Shanghai not talk about morality?" I think he was wrong. Cities originally don't have morality, especially Shanghai, which is a den of vice, where the word morality has long disappeared.

(3) Vase

The term "vase" was not widely heard in the first half of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Now, however, this name is all the rage. Newspapers carry it, and writers are also making an unexpected fortune with the term "vase." This term is probably a new invention in the literary world of the 21st year of the Republic of China. It is said that "vase" is a derogatory term for women, which may have some basis. Because women are as beautiful as flowers, calling them vases is not entirely inappropriate.

(4) Ideology Originally Did Not Exist

The purpose of the ×× ideology is to alleviate the suffering of the people, support labor, promote education for the poor, and protect the working class. Mr. S once joined the ×× ideology and was a loyal believer in the ×× ideology. Recently, Mr. S obtained a job at Company B, relying on the capitalist class, which was originally not allowed by the ×× ideology. After Mr. S entered Company B, he specialized in catering to his superiors and being harsh to the workers, completely changing his previous demeanor. What is the reason for this? I think ideology originally did not exist.

(5) Leaving Home and Abandoning Home

People must experience birth, death, separation, and parting. When the moment of parting with parents and loved ones comes, how sad it is, how reluctant one is to leave. However, as soon as one arrives at a certain place and falls in love with a woman, all the sadness and reluctance dissolve. It is not uncommon to not send a letter home for three years, as if one has no home but only remembers her.

Casual Notes from Stone Tower 227

— Kang Shi

(1) How Heartbreaking

On September 18th, Shenyang was forcibly occupied by Japanese pirates, leaving behind a scorched earth. On January 28th, Songhu suffered another tragic robbery by Japanese pirates, again leaving behind a scorched earth. Unexpectedly, just a few months later, the Lu war suddenly broke out, and Yexian was left in a scorched earth. But before one scene closed, another opened, with the Sichuan war, where Luzhou was also left in a scorched earth. Alas! In addition to the scorched earth of foreign troubles of "September 18th" and "January 28th," there is still scorched earth resulting from civil war. How heartbreaking!

"If people don't offend me, I won't offend them" is a common saying among warlords fighting for power and territory. But in the Sichuan-Lu war, who offended whom first? Launching such a major offensive, causing such widespread suffering. Consider: the Japanese pirates' invasion is "people offending me," but we don't "also offend people." Alas? In civil war, "people offend people" and "I also offend people." In foreign troubles, "people offend me" but "I don't offend people," and we don't resist at all. How heartbreaking!

(2) Commonplace

When unscrupulous merchants are warned by patriotic people, they initially restrain themselves a little, but now it has become "commonplace" and not surprising. Therefore, the warnings are given, but the unscrupulous merchants continue to do what they do. Alas! How painful! How hateful!

Although the Shanghai war ended many months ago, there are still many leftover explosives that frequently explode and injure people, as if warning compatriots not to forget the tragic situation of being ravaged by Japanese violence on "January 28th." However, as time passes, the repeated explosions that injure people have become "commonplace." Everyone is numb and indifferent, only blaming the carelessness of those who are hit, but not blaming the source of the poison—the Japanese pirates—for the gift to compatriots. Wake up, fellow countrymen!

(3) I Don't Have... Therefore...

I don't have money, so I am looked down upon and treated with contempt.

I don't have the skill to flatter, so I remain as I am.

I don't have the art of manipulating and winning, so I am even poorer.

I don't have the ability to scheme, so I remain a small businessman.

I don't have the ability to boast, so no one believes me.

I haven't gilded myself at universities and middle schools, so my friends despise me for being uneducated.

I don't have profound knowledge, so I can only resent the corruption of society, but I don't have good ways to save society.

Regulations for the Shop Assistants' Correspondence Column 228

(1) Purpose of Correspondence: The purpose of this column is to gather wisdom, explain difficult problems, sharpen each other, and increase the happiness of life.

(2) Target Audience: The target audience of this column is limited to shop assistants and apprentices, and geographically limited to this city.

(3) Content of Correspondence: All issues related to personal daily life, such as:

(1) Occupation (2) Moral and academic cultivation (3) Entertainment and sports (4) Marriage and other issues, as well as other issues related to the country and society, are all welcome.

If the content of the problem is too profound and beyond the ability of this column, it can also be referred to the "Reader Consultant" of this newspaper for answers.

(4) How to Submit Letters

(1) The name, age, native place, occupation, and detailed mailing address must be written at the end of the letter; this information must be continuously written in subsequent letters.

(2) The style of the letter is not limited, but it should be simple and easy to understand, and it must be written clearly.

(3) Please write "Shop Assistants' Correspondence Column, Shen Bao Newspaper, Local Edition" on the envelope; if a reply is required, please enclose a two-cent stamp.

(4) Correspondents must cut out the specially printed stamp for this column and paste it on the upper left corner of the letter; letters without the stamp will not be answered.

(5) Processing Method after Receiving Letters

(1) If this newspaper believes that the issues discussed are valuable to the public, they may be disclosed in the newspaper.

(2) To respect the opinions of correspondents, if a letter states that the correspondent does not wish to disclose their name or requires a separate reply, this can also be done.

(3) If a correspondent wishes to have their letter disclosed in the newspaper, but the length is too long and cannot be fully disclosed, excerpts will be published. Also, if the content of the problem is complex and requires careful study, which may result in a delayed answer or disclosure, readers are asked to forgive us.

(4) When there is a large number of letters, they will be answered in the order in which they are received, and any delays are hoped to be forgiven.

Novel

Written to a Friend's Wife 229

— Qin Jianou

This is a novel in the format of a letter, which is very popular in Europe and the United States right now. Indeed, I also feel that writing a self-narrative novel in this format is relatively more convenient and neat. And on the reader's side, they can, from a natural misidentification, believe that the freedom of the characters in the book evokes a deeper level of sympathy.

××:

Truly, although for the past two years, I have constantly held the hunger and thirst to write you a cheerful, sincere love letter, from the very beginning when this desire arose, I also felt the difficulty of writing this love letter. Indeed, today, on this most courageous day, when I picked up my pen, the first word encountered a strong obstacle. How should I address you? The two words "sister-in-law" seem to be the most suitable, but they are not appropriate for a love letter, nor is it what I want to write. Then, should I call you "Yingmei" or "Manying"? While that is certainly very affectionate, thinking of myself, I feel it is too risky. Perhaps your teasing me is purely unconscious, and there is no possibility of accepting such a passionate form of address from me!

"Unconscious teasing!" I have worried about this too! I have been terrified by this! But every time this illusion occurs, it is immediately broken by the most eloquent facts.

Now, after twenty-four months of trying and being close to you, even if someone uses the most solid evidence to tell me that the water in the Huangpu River is a mutated sweet spring, even if such an unbelievable fact occurs, I can no longer doubt that you have no sincere feelings for me!

"Contradiction! Contradiction!" After reading these three paragraphs of mine, you may laugh loudly and shout.

That's right, the sentences above and below are contradictory. But, my little friend, you must know that human nature is inherently contradictory. Especially when a man, full of suspicion and burning with the "fire of love," is preparing to pour out his heart to the ideal lover he "thinks of day and night," the more he wants to say it clearly and sincerely, the more confused and contradictory he becomes.

Let's use our affair as an example: logically speaking, you are the wife of my friend. "One should not flirt with a friend's wife!" This is a clear instruction from the ancients. I should know this, and I do know this. To be honest, I not only already know this, but judging from my usual words and deeds, I am the strongest opponent of "those who flirt with a friend's wife." I don't even want my friend to say a single word to my wife. But I have very actively seized you and made you my passionate opponent. I have tried every possible way to flirt with my friend's wife. Isn't this contradictory to the extreme?

It is already contradictory, but not only am I unwilling to correct this contradictory thought and eliminate this contradictory behavior, but I am also sincerely praying that this contradictory thought and contradictory behavior will continue. Even if I lose my lifelong reputation because of this, and abandon all that I have, I will never regret it; I am only quietly waiting for the arrival of death.

In fact, my dear little friend, during these two years, I have also been stimulated by morality and tried several times to squeeze out a kind of shameful repentance. Unfortunately, I am just an ordinary little businessman, and how can I have a wisdom sword? Naturally, I can't cut off this tough thread of love. Therefore, the time occupied by each repentance is only like a flash of lightning, lasting less than a few minutes, at most only one or two hours.

I remember March 13th, 19th year of the Republic of China, a spring evening two years ago. The weather was most suitable with a slight warmth. The French parasol trees on both sides of the concession road were competing to grow fresh green leaves. Every passing girl, wearing the new outfit she had just brought back from the department store window, draped it very fittingly over her slender and fleshy body, revealing an extremely excited attitude, very proudly carrying her own captive, in cars, in trams, on the sidewalks, heading in different directions. It was at this time that I, who had graduated from a university in the city and transformed into the principal of a county normal school, after spending seven months of lonely rural life, once again left my loving father, my virtuous but unsophisticated wife, my lively daughter, wearing the latest style of Western suit from 1930, striding towards this "skyscraper-cloud-transforming" Shanghai, coming excitedly.

My motivation for resolutely throwing myself into this scorching furnace for the second time was certainly not for you. Because at that time, I simply hadn't discovered that there was such a suspiciously beautiful woman like you in the world! I came to Shanghai purely to earn a few more dollars!

A monthly salary of two hundred and fifty-seven yuan, outwardly a general manager able to handle things alone. This was enough to make me happy to the point of forgetting my name. What's more, in addition to this superior position, there was another gratifying thing: my old classmate, your legal lover, Zhou Dajing, had also arrived in Shanghai a month earlier from Jinan.

Film Special

Overseas News

Hollywood's Livestock Agency 230

— Lin

Hollywood has recently discovered a livestock agency. This is a very novel type of business because this agency is fully equipped with all kinds of animals, large like elephants, small like mice, fierce like tigers, poisonous like snakes, and cunning like monkeys. Any kind of livestock needed by film companies can be called for by phone and will arrive in an instant. For example, if you need a polar bear tomorrow at ten o'clock, that can jump into the water from a platform twenty feet high, that can all be done.

The person who founded this agency has been engaged in training animals for the needs of various film studios for seven years. His name is Pat Healey. He is a man of few words and many deeds. In these past seven years, he has never failed to fulfill a request. The things that film companies demand from him are strange and unusual, not only birds and beasts, but also things like insects, but Healey is sure to find a way to gather them and not fail the trust.

Many people who demand things from Healey can be said to have no common sense. They often want a small lion, or a caterpillar, or a swallow, and don't think about whether these things are in season. Therefore, Healey's only job is to find ways to search in all directions for things that are not in season, no matter spring, summer, autumn, or winter. His representatives are all over the world, and the transportation methods used, such as ships, airplanes, trains, mail, etc., all strive for speed to please his customers. But Healey is not bothered by this, but thinks that the joy of the business is this point of "being able to do what others cannot."

But in fact, the things that Hollywood film studios usually need do not require much effort to find overseas. It is said that Hollywood is a very strange place. Hollywood can find almost everything in the world because there are many men and women around Hollywood who specialize in raising livestock for a living. All kinds of rare birds and exotic animals can be temporarily rented from the various farms. Each of them has their own specialties. Crocodiles, bears, monkeys, lions, ostriches, snakes, foxes, yellow birds, pigeons, owls, eagles, etc., can be rented from various families. There are also many monsters from the Classic of Mountains and Seas that can be borrowed from the agency.

Healey said: The current moviegoers are no longer the same as before. In the past, if something was missing, it could be replaced with something similar, but that is not possible now. Therefore, the work of the agency is especially heavy. The table listed below shows the daily rental prices for various common beasts:

Elephant: $100 Sea Dog: $35

Lion, Tiger, Leopard, Bear, etc.: $25

Monkey: $20 Snake: $15

House Cat: $0.75 Rabbit: $0.25

But these prices cannot be generalized. It also depends on their skills. For example, a dog costs $1.50 per day to rent, but if it is alert and can act, it costs $150 per day. Of course, Rin Tin Tin is not included in this example.

Dickie Moore 231

Child star Dickie Moore co-starred with big star John Barrymore in the movie The Beloved Rogue when he was less than one year old. He is now six years old and recently appeared with Marlene Dietrich in The Blonde Venus.

Little Commentary

Talking About Yuan Meiyun 232

— Rui Ying

Those who have seen "Little Actress" have probably already understood the skills of the fifteen-year-old child star Yuan Meiyun. All her expressions of joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness are revealed in her innocent expressions. It is heard that Yuan Meiyun previously performed on the Tianchan stage. Shao Zuiweng, the owner of Tianyi, appreciated her talent and specially wrote a script for her, inviting her to play the lead role. Yuan Meiyun did not disgrace her mission and was able to reveal her genius from the start. In "Little Actress," there are several scenes that can make people cry, such as the scene where she jumps up when she sees a figure outside the window at night, and the scene where she meets her mother upon returning home. How deeply they strike the hearts of the audience!

From now on, there will be one more Yuan Meiyun among the successful Chinese female stars!

— Ji Zhong

Young sister Li Minghui has been in Shanghai for several months since coming from Hong Kong. Due to Shao Zuiweng's vigorous persuasion and her father Jinhui's introduction, she formally joined Tianyi. But since joining, several weeks have passed, and the Tianyi authorities have still not written a script for Minghui to star in. Meanwhile, others such as Chen Yumei, Lu Lixia, and Yuan Meiyun have finished one play and are already continuing to shoot another. Minghui is accustomed to moving and not accustomed to being still. Recently, she has been doing nothing in her spare time. Her heart is truly depressed beyond description.

Film Review

The Valuation of Love 235

— Yan Nan

Most young people in love probably hope to know the valuation of love, right? In the new film "The Valuation of Love" by Guo Qin Ying, there is also no accurate answer given; it is still only vaguely said that love can be bought with no money. This is very much in line with the original drama title "Bought." But they are probably all thinking that love is just bought, so in the end, it still points out the disillusionment of buying love and the perfect union of pure love.

It mocks women's love of money and men's emphasis on social status, just like other love films, slandering vain love!

The plot is roughly about: an illegitimate daughter, living a self-reliant life, gets along well with a poor intellectual, but receives considerable help in material terms from an old gentleman. Soon, she meets a wealthy young man and leaves her old lover behind. When this young man learns that she is an illegitimate daughter, the engagement that the two sides had made is broken off. When she returns to the old gentleman's house, her old lover is already waiting for her. Only then does she understand that this wealthy gentleman is her biological father. In her reconciliation with her old lover and their mutual embrace, this play ends!

Constance Bennett, playing this naive and innocent girl just discovering love, is better than her previous performances. The two drunken scenes are wonderfully done. Originally a completely inexperienced woman, stepping onto the path of society, her various expressions—joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness—are not due to the heart. Constance plays this role, empathizing and being natural. Richard Bennett, playing the gentleman, is mature and dignified, inspiring awe. The real-life father and daughter, playing the fake father and daughter in the play, their dialogues and expressions are seamlessly connected, vividly portraying a pair of loving father and weak daughter. Perhaps this is due to nature. Ben Lyon, playing the writer, although not entirely suitable, still has admirable aspects, at least being able to talk about inner performance. Raymond Milland is indeed a handsome and healthy young man, revealing the personality of a playboy and spoiled young master. With his beauty, Hollywood can probably count on him. Perhaps the director is using his beauty as an object for women's vanity. The neatness of the supporting roles is something Warner Bros. has never done before.

The cooperation between the director and cinematographer has excellent results. The light is sometimes too bright (such as in the moonlit scenes, it would be more romantic if it were a little darker), but overall it is still good.

The small interludes and hidden writings are extremely beautiful, such as the shadow left behind when people leave, the smoke released by the pipe; the three birthday gifts, etc., all have the power to evoke memories. The comparison before and after is also very touching, invisibly expressing a kind of spiritual contradiction and material change.

However, the middle section could be shorter; and at the end, the woman's photo in the gentleman's study should be a close-up to attract the audience's attention, because the center of the comedy ultimately comes down to this photo!

A Discussion of Domestic Films

Another "Little Actress" 236

— Xing Su

No matter what kind of drama, film or stage play, its only creed is "playing a role without getting too into the role". "Little Actress" suffers from the problem of getting too into the role. The opening scene showing Wang's shrewishness seems to deviate from reason. Why describe the father-in-law and husband as so weak? If not hitting the father-in-law and not hitting the husband, is there no suitable and reasonable material in this life?

Little Lin's family is not that poor. We can see this from the set design. Otherwise, how could Wang have won the favor of Chen Naixin, who acts like he is tearing down walls? But Little Lin's grandfather, after falling on hard times, seems to have completely revealed the ugly side of a country bumpkin. How could he be so unaware of the world? Because the description is excessive, such a contradiction arises.

Little Lin is just a little actress who has just stepped onto the stage. How could she suddenly become so popular? And after that, Little Lin's teacher's wife disappears without a trace. This alone is enough to show that the screenwriter lacks too much understanding of life.

When Ji Zhong is sick with anger, Wang answers her lover's phone. Because Ji Zhong groans, she cannot hear the phone clearly and gets angry and scolds him. And this scene of Ji Zhong being thirsty in his illness is exactly the same as the treatment Wang receives from Chen Naixin when she is sick, without the slightest difference. It is clumsy and too stupid. Everyone can decide that in this world, there is no such identical parallel life.

The letter that Little Lin writes home has "Zhangjiabang, to be received by Mother" written on the envelope. The postman somehow knows the original address of the letter writer's mother and actually sends it to find her. When has there ever been such a clever postman? But the postman's cleverness is also the director's clumsiness.

The leading actress, Yuan Meiyun, is able to act and her performance is not bad. She is a promising talent, and this should not be buried.

Film Monographs

Practicing "Smiling Broadly" 237

— Chen Dabei

Let's put aside all kinds of infinitely changing smiles for now and first practice this most common and straightforward smile.

This is the sixth form of the Expression Self-Study Method. The method of practice is slightly different from the previous five forms. First, pay attention to the space between your eyebrows in the mirror. (Don't forget, your eyes must be more than a foot away from the mirror.) Then, while slowly counting "one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight" silently, slowly inhale a breath from your nose. At the same time, your mouth slowly opens into a smile, and your eyes slowly narrow, practicing the meaning of the four words "smiling broadly." By the time you finish counting eight words, you have just turned into a smiling face like Maitreya Buddha.

As before, while holding onto this breath and this smile, slowly count "one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight" silently (of course, without making a sound). At this time, you must pay close attention and keep this smile without the slightest change, as if you are facing a camera to leave a smiling photo. I know that many people cannot easily do this. Because they have never looked at themselves in the mirror with such a dignified appearance, and they will burst out laughing when they see it. This laugh is not a big deal, but it completely blows out the breath you were holding. Remember! When holding this smile, you must keep it without the slightest change.

Then gradually increase the degree of the smile. While silently counting "one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight" and exhaling this breath, your eyes narrow more and more, and your mouth opens more and more, smiling until the "eight" and you have smiled out all the air in your lungs, to the point where you cannot breathe.
